Pass --comment to post findings as inline PR comments, or --fix to apply the findings to the working tree after the review.\n- simplify: Review the changed code for reuse, simplification, efficiency, and altitude cleanups, then apply the fixes. Quality only — it does not hunt for bugs; use /code-review for that.\n- fewer-permission-prompts: Scan your transcripts for common read-only Bash and MCP tool calls, then add a prioritized allowlist to project .claude/settings.json to reduce permission prompts.\n- loop: Run a prompt or slash command on a recurring interval (e.g. /loop 5m /foo). {"parentUuid":"d3fd2393-1173-4171-9a7e-ac1048832569","isSidechain":true,"promptId":"ff6c8414-3cf8-4eac-9dd8-a003a75cddc1","agentId":"abafec4c377a11bdf","type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_015TU8M1F62kAREPgi1LtqqG","type":"tool_result","content":"1\t//! Outbound email provider adapter.\n2\t//!\n3\t//! Sends transactional email (e.g. the open-signup OTP) over SMTP via an\n4\t//! authenticated STARTTLS relay — the OCI Email Delivery endpoint in production.\n5\t//! TLS is provided by `lettre`'s bundled rustls backend (the workspace ships no\n6\t//! other TLS stack: `reqwest` is built `default-features = false`), so this crate\n7\t//! pulls `lettre` with `tokio1-rustls-tls` and nothing system-native.\n8\t//!\n9\t//! Mirrors the provider-adapter shape of `mnt-platform-push`: a `*Config` with a\n10\t//! `validate()`, an async sender trait, a live adapter, and a stub that degrades\n11\t//! gracefully when the integration is unconfigured.\n12\t#![cfg_attr(test, allow(clippy::unwrap_used, clippy::expect_used, clippy::panic))]\n13\t\n14\tuse std::future::Future;\n15\tuse std::pin::Pin;\n16\tuse std::time::Duration;\n17\t\n18\tuse lettre::transport::smtp::authentication::Credentials;\n19\tuse lettre::{AsyncSmtpTransport, AsyncTransport, Message, Tokio1Executor};\n20\t\n21\tpub type BoxFuture<'a, T> = Pin<Box<dyn Future<Output = T> + Send + 'a>>;\n22\t\n23\t#[derive(Debug, thiserror::Error)]\n24\tpub enum EmailError {\n25\t    #[error(\"invalid email configuration: {0}\")]\n26\t    Config(String),\n27\t\n28\t    #[error(\"failed to build email message: {0}\")]\n29\t    Message(String),\n30\t\n31\t    #[error(\"SMTP delivery failed: {0}\")]\n32\t    Transport(String),\n33\t}\n34\t\n35\t/// SMTP relay configuration for outbound transactional email.\n36\t///\n37\t/// In production these point at the OCI Email Delivery STARTTLS relay; the\n38\t/// `username`/`password` are the SMTP credentials issued for the approved\n39\t/// sender. Every field is required — a partially-configured relay is a\n40\t/// misconfiguration, surfaced by [`SmtpEmailConfig::validate`].\n41\t#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq)]\n42\tpub struct SmtpEmailConfig {\n43\t    pub host: String,\n44\t    pub port: u16,\n45\t    pub username: String,\n46\t    pub password: String,\n47\t    pub from_address: String,\n48\t    pub from_name: String,\n49\t}\n50\t\n51\timpl SmtpEmailConfig {\n52\t    pub fn validate(&self) -> Result<(), EmailError> {\n53\t        require_non_empty(&self.host, \"SMTP host\")?;\n54\t        if self.port == 0 {\n55\t            return Err(EmailError::Config(\"SMTP port is required\".to_owned()));\n56\t        }\n57\t        require_non_empty(&self.username, \"SMTP username\")?;\n58\t        require_non_empty(&self.password, \"SMTP password\")?;\n59\t        require_non_empty(&self.from_address, \"email from address\")?;\n60\t        require_non_empty(&self.from_name, \"email from name\")\n61\t    }\n62\t}\n63\t\n64\t/// Outbound transactional email port. Async by way of `BoxFuture` so the trait\n65\t/// stays object-safe behind `Arc<dyn EmailSender>` (mirrors `PushNotifier`).\n66\tpub trait EmailSender: Send + Sync {\n67\t    /// Send a one-time-passcode email to `to`. `ttl` is rendered into the body so\n68\t    /// the recipient knows how long the code is valid.\n69\t    fn send_otp<'a>(\n70\t        &'a self,\n71\t        to: &'a str,\n72\t        code: &'a str,\n73\t        ttl: Duration,\n74\t    ) -> BoxFuture<'a, Result<(), EmailError>>;\n75\t}\n76\t\n77\t/// Live SMTP sender over an authenticated STARTTLS relay (OCI Email Delivery).\n78\t#[derive(Clone)]\n79\tpub struct LettreSmtpSender {\n80\t    config: SmtpEmailConfig,\n81\t    transport: AsyncSmtpTransport<Tokio1Executor>,\n82\t}\n83\t\n84\timpl LettreSmtpSender {\n85\t    pub fn new(config: SmtpEmailConfig) -> Result<Self, EmailError> {\n86\t        config.validate()?;\n87\t        let transport = AsyncSmtpTransport::<Tokio1Executor>::starttls_relay(&config.host)\n88\t            .map_err(|err| EmailError::Config(err.to_string()))?\n89\t            .port(config.port)\n90\t            .credentials(Credentials::new(\n91\t                config.username.clone(),\n92\t                config.password.clone(),\n93\t            ))\n94\t            .build();\n95\t        Ok(Self { config, transport })\n96\t    }\n97\t}\n98\t\n99\timpl EmailSender for LettreSmtpSender {\n100\t    fn send_otp<'a>(\n101\t        &'a self,\n102\t        to: &'a str,\n103\t        code: &'a str,\n104\t        ttl: Duration,\n105\t    ) -> BoxFuture<'a, Result<(), EmailError>> {\n106\t        Box::pin(async move {\n107\t            let from = format!(\"{} <{}>\", self.config.from_name, self.config.from_address);\n108\t            let message =\n109\t                Message::builder()\n110\t                    .from(from.parse().map_err(|err| {\n111\t                        EmailError::Message(format!(\"invalid from address: {err}\"))\n112\t                    })?)\n113\t                    .to(to.parse().map_err(|err| {\n114\t                        EmailError::Message(format!(\"invalid recipient address: {err}\"))\n115\t                    })?)\n116\t                    .subject(\"Your verification code\")\n117\t                    .body(otp_body(code, ttl))\n118\t                    .map_err(|err| EmailError::Message(err.to_string()))?;\n119\t            self.transport\n120\t                .send(message)\n121\t                .await\n122\t                .map_err(|err| EmailError::Transport(err.to_string()))?;\n123\t            Ok(())\n124\t        })\n125\t    }\n126\t}\n127\t\n128\t/// Stub sender used when SMTP is Outbound email provider adapter.\n//!\n//! Sends transactional email (e.g. the open-signup OTP) over SMTP via an\n//! authenticated STARTTLS relay — the OCI Email Delivery endpoint in production.\n//! TLS is provided by `lettre`'s bundled rustls backend (the workspace ships no\n//! other TLS stack: `reqwest` is built `default-features = false`), so this crate\n//! pulls `lettre` with `tokio1-rustls-tls` and nothing system-native.\n//!\n//! Mirrors the provider-adapter shape of `mnt-platform-push`: a `*Config` with a\n//! `validate()`, an async sender trait, a live adapter, and a stub that degrades\n//! gracefully when the integration is unconfigured.\n#![cfg_attr(test, allow(clippy::unwrap_used, clippy::expect_used, clippy::panic))]\n\nuse std::future::Future;\nuse std::pin::Pin;\nuse std::time::Duration;\n\nuse lettre::transport::smtp::authentication::Credentials;\nuse lettre::{AsyncSmtpTransport, AsyncTransport, Message, Tokio1Executor};\n\npub type BoxFuture<'a, T> = Pin<Box<dyn Future<Output = T> + Send + 'a>>;\n\n#[derive(Debug, thiserror::Error)]\npub enum EmailError {\n    #[error(\"invalid email configuration: {0}\")]\n    Config(String),\n\n    #[error(\"failed to build email message: {0}\")]\n    Message(String),\n\n    #[error(\"SMTP delivery failed: {0}\")]\n    Transport(String),\n}\n\n/// SMTP relay configuration for outbound transactional email.\n///\n/// In production these point at the OCI Email Delivery STARTTLS relay; the\n/// `username`/`password` are the SMTP credentials issued for the approved\n/// sender. Every field is required — a partially-configured relay is a\n/// misconfiguration, surfaced by [`SmtpEmailConfig::validate`].\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq)]\npub struct SmtpEmailConfig {\n    pub host: String,\n    pub port: u16,\n    pub username: String,\n    pub password: String,\n    pub from_address: String,\n    pub from_name: String,\n}\n\nimpl SmtpEmailConfig {\n    pub fn validate(&self) -> Result<(), EmailError> {\n        require_non_empty(&self.host, \"SMTP host\")?;\n        if self.port == 0 {\n            return Err(EmailError::Config(\"SMTP port is required\".to_owned()));\n        }\n        require_non_empty(&self.username, \"SMTP username\")?;\n        require_non_empty(&self.password, \"SMTP password\")?;\n        require_non_empty(&self.from_address, \"email from address\")?;\n        require_non_empty(&self.from_name, \"email from name\")\n    }\n}\n\n/// Outbound transactional email port. Async by way of `BoxFuture` so the trait\n/// stays object-safe behind `Arc<dyn EmailSender>` (mirrors `PushNotifier`).\npub trait EmailSender: Send + Sync {\n    /// Send a one-time-passcode email to `to`. `ttl` is rendered into the body so\n    /// the recipient knows how long the code is valid.\n    fn send_otp<'a>(\n        &'a self,\n        to: &'a str,\n        code: &'a str,\n        ttl: Duration,\n    ) -> BoxFuture<'a, Result<(), EmailError>>;\n}\n\n/// Live SMTP sender over an authenticated STARTTLS relay (OCI Email Delivery).\n#[derive(Clone)]\npub struct LettreSmtpSender {\n    config: SmtpEmailConfig,\n    transport: AsyncSmtpTransport<Tokio1Executor>,\n}\n\nimpl LettreSmtpSender {\n    pub fn new(config: SmtpEmailConfig) -> Result<Self, EmailError> {\n        config.validate()?;\n        let transport = AsyncSmtpTransport::<Tokio1Executor>::starttls_relay(&config.host)\n            .map_err(|err| EmailError::Config(err.to_string()))?\n            .port(config.port)\n            .credentials(Credentials::new(\n                config.username.clone(),\n                config.password.clone(),\n            ))\n            .build();\n        Ok(Self { config, transport })\n    }\n}\n\nimpl EmailSender for LettreSmtpSender {\n    fn send_otp<'a>(\n        &'a self,\n        to: &'a str,\n        code: &'a str,\n        ttl: Duration,\n    ) -> BoxFuture<'a, Result<(), EmailError>> {\n        Box::pin(async move {\n            let from = format!(\"{} <{}>\", self.config.from_name, self.config.from_address);\n            let message =\n                Message::builder()\n                    .from(from.parse().map_err(|err| {\n                        EmailError::Message(format!(\"invalid from address: {err}\"))\n                    })?)\n                    .to(to.parse().map_err(|err| {\n                        EmailError::Message(format!(\"invalid recipient address: {err}\"))\n                    })?)\n                    .subject(\"Your verification code\")\n                    .body(otp_body(code, ttl))\n                    .map_err(|err| EmailError::Message(err.to_string()))?;\n            self.transport\n                .send(message)\n                .await\n                .map_err(|err| EmailError::Transport(err.to_string()))?;\n            Ok(())\n        })\n    }\n}\n\n/// Stub sender used when SMTP is unconfigured. Logs the OTP via `tracing` and\n/// returns `Ok(())` — it NEVER sends mail. Mirrors how the Solapi/FCM adapters\n/// degrade when their credentials are absent, so the app boots and local/dev\n/// flows can read the code from the logs.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Default)]\npub struct StubEmailSender;\n\nimpl EmailSender for StubEmailSender {\n    fn send_otp<'a>(\n        &'a self,\n        to: &'a str,\n        code: &'a str,\n        ttl: Duration,\n    ) -> BoxFuture<'a, Result<(), EmailError>> {\n        Box::pin(async move {\n            tracing::info!(target: \"mnt::email\", \"[DEV] OTP for {to}: {code} (ttl {ttl:?})\");\n            Ok(())\n        })\n    }\n}\n\nfn otp_body(code: &str, ttl: Duration) -> String {\n    let minutes = ttl.as_secs() / 60;\n    format!(\n        \"Your verification code is {code}.\\n\\nIt expires in {minutes} minutes.\\n\\nIf you did not request this, you can ignore this email.\\n\"\n    )\n}\n\nfn require_non_empty(value: &str, name: &str) -> Result<(), EmailError> {\n    if value.trim().is_empty() {\n        Err(EmailError::Config(format!(\"{name} is required\")))\n    } else {\n        Ok(())\n    }\n}\n\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod tests {\n    use super::*;\n\n    fn valid_config() -> SmtpEmailConfig {\n        SmtpEmailConfig {\n            host: \"smtp.email.ap-chuncheon-1.oci.oraclecloud.com\".to_owned(),\n            port: 587,\n            username: \"ocid1.user.oc1..example\".to_owned(),\n            password: \"secret\".to_owned(),\n            from_address: \"noreply@example.com\".to_owned(),\n            from_name: \"MNT\".to_owned(),\n        }\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn valid_config_passes_validation() {\n        assert!(valid_config().validate().is_ok());\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn validate_rejects_empty_host() {\n        let mut config = valid_config();\n        config.host = String::new();\n        assert!(config.validate().is_err());\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn validate_rejects_zero_port() {\n        let mut config = valid_config();\n        config.port = \"conflict\", err.message)\n284\t            }\n285\t            ErrorKind::Internal => {\n286\t                Self::new(StatusCode::INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR, \"internal\", err.message)\n287\t            }\n288\t        }\n289\t    }\n290\t\n291\t    fn from_store(err: PgMessengerError) -> Self {\n292\t        match err {\n293\t            PgMessengerError::Domain(err) => disclosure, OWASP A05). Clients get a stable message.\n297\t                tracing::error!(error = %err, \"database error\");\n298\t                Self::new(\n299\t Result<ThreadSummary, PgMessengerError> {\n142\t        if let Some(existing) =\n143\t            fetch_work_order_thread_pool(&self.pool, command.work_order_id).await?\n144\t        {\n145\t            return Ok(existing);\n146\t        }\n147\t\n148\t        let request_no = work_order_request_no(&self.pool, command.work_order_id).await?;\n149\t        ensure_work_order_branch_pool(&self.pool, command.work_order_id, command.branch_id).await?;\n150\t        let thread_id = ThreadId::new();\n151\t        let org = current_org().map_err(KernelError::from)?;\n152\t        let org_uuid = *org.as_uuid();\n153\t        let event = messenger_audit_event(\n154\t            \"message_thread.create\",\n155\t            command.actor,\n156\t            command.branch_id,\n157\t            \"message_thread\",\n158\t            thread_id,\n159\t            command.trace,\n160\t            command.occurred_at,\n161\t        )?\n162\t        .with_org(org);\n163\t        let title = format!(\"WO {request_no}\");\n164\t\n165\t        let result = with_audit::<_, ThreadSummary, PgMessengerError>(&self.pool, event, |tx| {\n166\t            Box::pin(async move {\n167\t                insert_thread_tx(\n168\t                    tx,\n169\t                    NewThread {\n170\t                        id: thread_id,\n171\t                        kind: ThreadKind::WorkOrder,\n172\t                        branch_id: command.branch_id,\n173\t                        work_order_id: Some(command.work_order_id),\n174\t                        title: Some(&title),\n175\t                        actor: command.actor,\n176\t                        occurred_at: command.occurred_at,\n177\t                    },\n178\t                    &[command.actor],\n179\t                    org_uuid,\n180\t                )\n181\t                .await?;\n182\t                fetch_thread_summary_tx(tx, thread_id).await\n183\t            })\n184\t        })\n185\t        .await;\n186\t\n187\t        match result {\n188\t            Ok(summary) => Ok(summary),\n189\t            Err(err) if err.kind() == ErrorKind::Conflict => {\n190\t                fetch_work_order_thread_pool(&self.pool, command.work_order_id)\n191\t                    .await?\n192\t                    .ok_or_else(|| {\n193\t                        KernelError::conflict(\"work-order messenger thread create raced\").into()\n194\t                    })\n195\t            }\n196\t            Err(err) => Err(err),\n197\t        }\n198\t    }\n199\t\n200\t    pub async fn send_message(\n201\t        &self,\n202\t        command: SendMessageCommand,\n203\t    ) -> Result<MessageSummary, PgMessengerError> {\n204\t        let body = MessageBody::new(command.body)?;\n205\t        let access = require_thread_access(\n206\t            &self.pool,\n207\t            command.thread_id,\n208\t            command.actor,\n209\t            &command.branch_scope,\n210\t        )\n211\t        .await?;\n212\t        let message_id = MessageId::new();\n213\t        let attachment_ids = command.attachment_evidence_ids;\n214\t        let org command.actor,\n219\t            access.branch_id,\n220\t            \"message\",\n221\t            message_id,\n222\t            command.trace,\n223\t            command.occurred_at,\n224\t        \"sender_id\": command.actor,\n231\t                \"attachment_count\": attachment_ids.len(),\n232\t            })),\n233\t        );\n234\t\n235\t        let summary = with_audit::<_, MessageSummary, PgMessengerError>(&self.pool, event, |tx| {\n236\t            Box::pin(async move {\n237\t                sqlx::query(\n238\t                    r#\"\n239\t                        INSERT INTO messenger_messages (\n240\t                            id, thread_id, branch_id, sender_id, body, sent_at, created_at, org_id\n241\t                        )\n242\t                        VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6, $6, $7)\n243\t                        \"#,\n244\t                )\n245\t                .bind(*message_id.as_uuid())\n246\t                .bind(*command.thread_id.as_uuid())\n247\t                .bind(*access.branch_id.as_uuid())\n248\t                .bind(*command.actor.as_uuid())\n249\t                .bind(body.as_str())\n250\t                .bind(command.occurred_at)\n251\t                .bind(org_uuid)\n252\t                .execute(tx.as_mut())\n253\t                .await?;\n254\t\n255\t                for (index, evidence_id) in attachment_ids.iter().enumerate() {\n256\t                    let sort_order = i16::try_from(index + 1)\n257\t                        .map_err(|_| KernelError::validation(\"too many message attachments\"))?;\n258\t                    sqlx::query(\n259\t                        r#\"\n260\t                            INSERT INTO messenger_message_attachments (\n261\t                                message_id, evidence_id, sort_order, org_id\n262\t                            )\n263\t                            VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4)\n264\t                            \"#,\n265\t                    )\n266\t                    .bind(*message_id.as_uuid())\n267\t                    .bind(*evidence_id.as_uuid())\n268\t                    .bind(sort_order)\n269\t                    .bind(org_uuid)\n270\t                    .execute(tx.as_mut())\n271\t                    .await?;\n272\t                }\n273\t\n274\t                sqlx::query(\"UPDATE messenger_threads SET updated_at = $2 WHERE id = $1\")\n275\t                    .bind(*command.thread_id.as_uuid())\n276\t                    .bind(command.occurred_at)\n277\t                    .execute(tx.as_mut())\n278\t                    .await?;\n279\t\n280\t                fetch_message_summary_tx(tx, message_id).await\n281\t            })\n282\t        })\n283\t        .await?;\n284\t\n285\t        if let Some(notifier) = &self.notifier {\n286\t            notifier\n287\t                .message_posted(MessagePostedNotification {\n288\t                    message_id: summary.id,\n289\t                    thread_id: summary.thread_id,\n290\t                    branch_id: summary.branch_id,\n291\t                })\n292\t                .await;\n293\t        }\n294\t\n295\t        Ok(summary)\n296\t    }\n297\t\n298\t    /// Coalesce read receipts at the thread/user level and audit one\n299\t    /// `message.read` event per explicit read command rather than per message.\n300\t    /// That preserves who acknowledged which latest message while avoiding an\n301\t    /// audit row explosion for long catch-up pages.\n302\t    pub async fn mark_thread_read(\n303\t        &self,\n304\t        command: MarkThreadReadCommand,\n305\t    ) -> Result<ReadReceiptSummary, PgMessengerError> {\n306\t        let access = require_thread_access(\n307\t            &self.pool,\n308\t            command.thread_id,\n309\t            command.actor,\n310\t            &command.branch_scope,\n311\t        )\n312\t        .await?;\n313\t        ensure_message_in_thread_pool(&self.pool, command.last_read_message_id, command.thread_id)\n314\t            .await?;\n315\t        let org = current_org().map_err(KernelError::from)?;\n316\t        let org_uuid = *org.as_uuid();\n317\t        let event = messenger_audit_event(\n318\t            \"message.read\",\n319\t            command.actor,\n320\t            access.branch_id,\n321\t            \"message_thread\",\n322\t            command.thread_id,\n323\t            command.trace,\n324\t            command.occurred_at,\n325\t        )?\n326\t        .with_org(org)\n327\t        .with_snapshots(\n328\t            None,\n329\t            Some(serde_json::json!({\n330\t                \"last_read_message_id\": command.last_read_message_id,\n331\t            })),\n332\t        );\n333\t\n334\t        with_audit::<_, ReadReceiptSummary, PgMessengerError>(&self.pool, event, |tx| {\n335\t            Box::pin(async move {\n336\t                sqlx::query(\n337\t                    r#\"\n338\t                    INSERT INTO messenger_read_receipts (\n339\t                        thread_id, user_id, last_read_message_id, read_at, updated_at, org_id\n340\t                    )\n341\t                    VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $4, $5)\n342\t                    ON CONFLICT (thread_id, user_id) DO UPDATE\n343\t                    SET last_read_message_id = EXCLUDED.last_read_message_id,\n344\t                        read_at = EXCLUDED.read_at,\n345\t                        updated_at = EXCLUDED.updated_at\n346\t                    \"#,\n347\t                )\n348\t                .bind(*command.thread_id.as_uuid())\n349\t                .bind(*command.actor.as_uuid())\n350\t                .bind(*command.last_read_message_id.as_uuid())\n351\t                .bind(command.occurred_at)\n352\t                .bind(org_uuid)\n353\t                .execute(tx.as_mut())\n354\t                .await?;\n355\t                fetch_read_receipt_tx(tx, command.thread_id, command.actor).await\n356\t            })\n357\t        })\n358\t        .await\n359\t    }\n360\t\n361\t    pub async fn list_threads(\n362\t        &self,\n363\t        query: ListThreadsQuery,\n364\t    ) -> Result<Vec<ThreadSummary>, PgMessengerError> {\n365\t        let limit = normalized_limit(query.limit);\n366\t        let mut builder = QueryBuilder::<Postgres>::new(\n367\t            r#\"\n368\t            SELECT t.id, t.kind, t.branch_id, t.work_order_id, t.title,\n369\t                   t.created_at, t.updated_at,\n370\t                   lm.id AS last_message_id,\n371\t                   lm.sent_at AS last_message_at,\n372\t                   COUNT(tm_all.user_id)::BIGINT AS member_count\n373\t            FROM messenger_threads t\n374\t            JOIN messenger_thread_members tm_actor\n375\t              ON tm_actor.thread_id = t.id\n376\t             AND tm_actor.user_id =\n377\t            \"#,\n378\t        );\n379\t        builder.push_bind(*query.actor.as_uuid());\n380\t        builder.push(\n381\t            r#\"\n382\t            LEFT JOIN LATERAL (\n383\t                SELECT id, sent_at\n384\t                FROM messenger_messages\n385\t                WHERE thread_id = t.id\n386\t                ORDER BY sent_at DESC, id DESC\n387\t                LIMIT 1\n388\t            ) lm ON true\n389\t            LEFT JOIN messenger_thread_members tm_all ON tm_all.thread_id = t.id\n390\t            WHERE true\n391\t            \"#,\n392\t        );\n393\t        push_scope_filter(&mut builder, \"t.branch_id\", &query.branch_scope)?;\n394\t        builder.push(\n395\t            r#\"\n396\t            GROUP BY t.id, lm.id, lm.sent_at\n397\t            ORDER BY COALESCE(lm.sent_at, t.updated_at) DESC, t.id DESC\n398\t            LIMIT\n399\t            \"#,\n400\t        );\n401\t        builder.push_bind(limit);\n402\t\n403\t        let org = current_org().map_err(KernelError::from)?;\n404\t        let rows = with_org_conn::<_, _, PgMessengerError>(&self.pool, org, move |tx| {\n405\t            Box::pin(async move { Ok(builder.build().fetch_all(tx.as_mut()).await?) })\n406\t        })\n407\t        .await?;\n408\t        rows.iter().map(thread_summary_from_row).collect()\n409\t    }\n410\t\n411\t    pub async fn message_page(\n412\t        &self,\n413\t        query: MessagePageQuery,\n414\t    ) -> Result<MessagePage, PgMessengerError> {\n415\t        require_thread_access(\n416\t            &self.pool,\n417\t            query.thread_id,\n418\t            query.actor,\n419\t            &query.branch_scope,\n420\t        )\n421\t        .await?;\n422\t        let limit = normalized_limit(query.limit);\n423\t        let page_limit = limit + 1;\n424\t        let before = match query.before_message_id {\n425\t            Some(message_id) => {\n426\t                Some(message_cursor(&self.pool, message_id, query.thread_id).await?)\n427\t            }\n428\t            None => None,\n429\t        };\n430\t\n431\t        let mut builder = message_select_builder();\n432\t        builder.push(\" WHERE m.thread_id = \");\n433\t        builder.push_bind(*query.thread_id.as_uuid());\n434\t        if let Some((sent_at, id)) = before {\n435\t            builder.push(\" AND (m.sent_at, m.id) < (\");\n436\t            builder.push_bind(sent_at);\n437\t            builder.push(\", \");\n438\t            builder.push_bind(id);\n439\t            builder.push(\")\");\n440\t        }\n441\t        builder.push(\" GROUP BY m.id, sender.display_name ORDER BY m.sent_at DESC, m.id DESC LIMIT \");\n442\t        builder.push_bind(page_limit);\n443\t\n444\t        let org = current_org().map_err(KernelError::from)?;\n445\t        let rows = with_org_conn::<_, _, PgMessengerError>(&self.pool, org, move |tx| {\n446\t            Box::pin(async move { Ok(builder.build().fetch_all(tx.as_mut()).await?) })\n447\t        })\n448\t        .await?;\n449\t        let mut items: Vec<MessageSummary> = rows\n450\t            .iter()\n451\t            .map(message_summary_from_row)\n452\t            .collect::<Result<_, _>>()?;\n453\t        let has_more = i64::try_from(items.len()).unwrap_or(0) > limit;\n454\t        if has_more {\n455\t            let _ = items.pop();\n456\t        }\n457\t        let next_cursor = if has_more {\n458\t            items.last().map(|message| message.id)\n459\t        } else {\n460\t            None\n461\t        };\n462\t\n463\t        Ok(MessagePage { items, next_cursor })\n464\t    }\n465\t\n466\t    /// Search primarily uses the `search_vector` GIN index. PostgreSQL's\n467\t    /// built-in `simple` configuration has limited Korean tokenization without\n468\t    /// a mecab-style dictionary, so this T3.1 slice also applies an `ILIKE`\n469\t    /// substring fallback for Korean terms. That keeps polling search useful\n470\t    /// without pretending the FTS stack is linguistically complete.\n471\t    pub async fn search_messages(\n472\t        &self,\n473\t        query: SearchMessagesQuery,\n474\t    ) -> Result<Vec<MessageSummary>, PgMessengerError> {\n475\t        let search = query.query.trim();\n476\t        if search.is_empty() {\n477\t            return Err(KernelError::validation(\"search query is required\").into());\n478\t        }\n479\t        let limit = normalized_limit(query.limit);\n480\t        let mut builder = message_select_builder();\n481\t        builder.push(\n482\t            r#\"\n483\t            JOIN messenger_thread_members tm_actor\n484\t              ON tm_actor.thread_id = m.thread_id\n485\t             AND tm_actor.user_id =\n486\t            \"#,\n487\t        );\n488\t        builder.push_bind(*query.actor.as_uuid());\n489\t        builder.push(\" WHERE (m.search_vector @@ plainto_tsquery('simple', \");\n490\t        builder.push_bind(search);\n491\t        builder.push(\") OR m.body ILIKE \");\n492\t        builder.push_bind(format!(\"%{search}%\"));\n493\t        builder.push(\")\");\n494\t        push_scope_filter(&mut builder, \"m.branch_id\", &query.branch_scope)?;\n495\t        builder.push(\" GROUP BY m.id, sender.display_name ORDER BY m.sent_at DESC, m.id DESC LIMIT \");\n496\t        builder.push_bind(limit);\n497\t\n498\t        let org = current_org().map_err(KernelError::from)?;\n499\t        let rows = with_org_conn::<_, _, PgMessengerError>(&self.pool, org, move |tx| {\n500\t            Box::pin(async move { Ok(builder.build().fetch_all(tx.as_mut()).await?) })\n501\t        })\n502\t        .await?;\n503\t        rows.iter().map(message_summary_from_row).collect()\n504\t    }\n505\t}\n506\t\n507\timpl WorkOrderCreatedListener for PgMessengerStore {\n508\t    fn work_order_created(&self, event: WorkOrderCreatedEvent) -> WorkOrderCreatedFuture<'_> {\n509\t        Box::pin(async move {\n510\t            self.ensure_work_order_thread(EnsureWorkOrderThreadCommand {\n511\t                actor: event.actor,\n512\t                branch_id: event.branch_id,\n513\t                work_order_id: event.work_order_id,\n514\t                trace: event.trace,\n515\t                occurred_at: event.occurred_at,\n516\t            })\n517\t            .await\n518\t            .map(|_| ())\n519\t            .map_err(kernel_error_from_messenger_error)\n520\t        })\n521\t    }\n522\t}\n523\t\n524\t#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy)]\n525\tstruct ThreadAccess {\n526\t    branch_id: BranchId,\n527\t}\n528\t\n529\t#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy)]\n530\tstruct NewThread<'a> {\n531\t    id: ThreadId,\n532\t    kind: ThreadKind,\n533\t    branch_id: BranchId,\n534\t    work_order_id: Option<WorkOrderId>,\n535\t    title: Option<&'a str>,\n536\t    actor: UserId,\n537\t    occurred_at: time::OffsetDateTime,\n538\t}\n539\t\n540\tfn validate_thread_shape(command: &CreateThreadCommand) -> Result<(), PgMessengerError> {\n541\t    match command.kind {\n542\t        ThreadKind::WorkOrder if command.work_order_id.is_none() => Err(KernelError::validation(\n543\t            \"work-order messenger thread requires work_order_id\",\n544\t        )\n545\t        .into()),\n546\t        ThreadKind::WorkOrder => Ok(()),\n547\t        ThreadKind::Team | ThreadKind::Dm | ThreadKind::Group\n548\t            if command.work_order_id.is_some() =>\n549\t        {\n550\t            Err(KernelError::validation(\n551\t                \"only work-order messenger threads may carry work_order_id\",\n552\t            )\n553\t            .into())\n554\t        }\n555\t        ThreadKind::Dm if normalized_members(command.actor, &command.member_ids)?.len() != 2 => {\n556\t            Err(KernelError::validation(\"DM thread requires exactly two members\").into())\n557\t        }\n558\t        ThreadKind::Group if normalized_members(command.actor, &command.member_ids)?.len() < 3 => {\n559\t            Err(KernelError::validation(\"group thread requires at least three members\").into())\n560\t        }\n561\t        _ => Ok(()),\n562\t    }\n563\t}\n564\t\n565\tfn normalized_members(actor: UserId, members: &[UserId]) -> Result<Vec<UserId>, PgMessengerError> {\n566\t    let mut members = members.to_vec();\n567\t    members.push(actor);\n568\t    members.sort();\n569\t    members.dedup();\n570\t    if members.is_empty() {\n571\t        return Err(KernelError::validation(\"messenger thread requires members\").into());\n572\t    }\n573\t    Ok(members)\n574\t}\n575\t\n576\tfn ensure_branch_scope(scope: &BranchScope, branch_id: BranchId) -> Result<(), PgMessengerError> {\n577\t    if scope.allows(branch_id) {\n578\t        Ok(())\n579\t    } else {\n580\t        Err(KernelError::forbidden(\"messenger branch is outside principal scope\").into())\n581\t    }\n582\t}\n583\t\n584\tfn normalized_limit(limit: i64) -> i64 {\n585\t    limit.clamp(1, 100)\n586\t}\n587\t\n588\tasync fn insert_thread_tx(\n589\t    tx: &mut Transaction<'_, Postgres>,\n590\t    thread: NewThread<'_>,\n591\t    member_ids: &[UserId],\n592\t    org_uuid: uuid::Uuid,\n593\t) -> Result<(), PgMessengerError> {\n594\t    sqlx::query(\n595\t        r#\"\n596\t        INSERT INTO messenger_threads (\n597\t            id, kind, branch_id, work_order_id, title, created_by, created_at, updated_at, org_id\n598\t        )\n599\t        VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6, $7, $7, $8)\n600\t        \"#,\n601\t    )\n602\t    .bind(*thread.id.as_uuid())\n603\t    .bind(thread.kind.as_db_str())\n604\t    .bind(*thread.branch_id.as_uuid())\n605\t    .bind(thread.work_order_id.map(|id| *id.as_uuid()))\n606\t    .bind(thread.title)\n607\t    .bind(*thread.actor.as_uuid())\n608\t    .bind(thread.occurred_at)\n609\t    .bind(org_uuid)\n610\t    .execute(tx.as_mut())\n611\t    .await?;\n612\t\n613\t    for member_id in member_ids {\n614\t        let role = if *member_id == thread.actor {\n615\t            \"OWNER\"\n616\t        } else {\n617\t            \"MEMBER\"\n618\t        };\n619\t        sqlx::query(\n620\t            r#\"\n621\t            INSERT INTO messenger_thread_members (thread_id, user_id, role, joined_at, org_id)\n622\t            VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5)\n623\t            ON CONFLICT (thread_id, user_id) DO NOTHING\n624\t            \"#,\n625\t        )\n626\t        .bind(*thread.id.as_uuid())\n627\t        .bind(*member_id.as_uuid())\n628\t        .bind(role)\n629\t        .bind(thread.occurred_at)\n630\t        .bind(org_uuid)\n631\t        .execute(tx.as_mut())\n632\t        .await?;\n633\t    }\n634\t\n635\t    Ok(())\n636\t}\n637\t\n638\tasync fn require_thread_access(\n639\t    pool: &PgPool,\n640\t    thread_id: ThreadId,\n641\t    actor: UserId,\n642\t    branch_scope: &BranchScope,\n643\t) -> Result<ThreadAccess, PgMessengerError> {\n644\t    let org = current_org().map_err(KernelError::from)?;\n645\t    let row = with_org_conn::<_, _, PgMessengerError>(pool, org, move |tx| {\n646\t        Box::pin(async move {\n647\t            Ok(sqlx::query(\n648\t                r#\"\n649\t        SELECT t.branch_id,\n650\t               EXISTS (\n651\t                   SELECT 1\n652\t                   FROM messenger_thread_members tm\n653\t                   WHERE tm.thread_id = t.id\n654\t                     AND tm.user_id = $2\n655\t               ) AS is_member\n656\t        FROM messenger_threads t\n657\t        WHERE t.id = $1\n658\t        \"#,\n659\t            )\n660\t            .bind(*thread_id.as_uuid())\n661\t            .bind(*actor.as_uuid())\n662\t            .fetch_optional(tx.as_mut())\n663\t            .await?)\n664\t        })\n665\t    })\n666\t    .await?\n667\t    .ok_or_else(|| KernelError::not_found(\"messenger thread was not found\"))?;\n668\t\n669\t    let branch_id = BranchId::from_uuid(row.try_get(\"branch_id\")?);\n670\t    ensure_branch_scope(branch_scope, branch_id)?;\n671\t    let is_member: bool = row\n672\t        .try_get::<Option<bool>, _>(\"is_member\")?\n673\t        .unwrap_or(false);\n674\t    if !is_member {\n675\t        return Err(KernelError::forbidden(\"actor is not a messenger thread member\").into());\n676\t    }\n677\t    Ok(ThreadAccess { branch_id })\n678\t}\n679\t\n680\tasync fn ensure_work_order_branch_pool(\n681\t    pool: &PgPool,\n682\t    work_order_id: WorkOrderId,\n683\t    branch_id: BranchId,\n684\t) -> Result<(), PgMessengerError> {\n685\t    let org = current_org().map_err(KernelError::from)?;\n686\t    let actual: uuid::Uuid = with_org_conn::<_, _, PgMessengerError>(pool, org, move |tx| {\n687\t        Box::pin(async move {\n688\t            Ok(\n689\t                sqlx::query_scalar(\"SELECT branch_id FROM work_orders WHERE id = $1\")\n690\t                    .bind(*work_order_id.as_uuid())\n691\t                    .fetch_optional(tx.as_mut())\n692\t                    .await?,\n693\t            )\n694\t        })\n695\t    })\n696\t    .await?\n697\t    .ok_or_else(|| KernelError::not_found(\"work order was not found\"))?;\n698\t    if actual == *branch_id.as_uuid() {\n699\t        Ok(())\n700\t    } else {\n701\t        Err(KernelError::forbidden(\"work order belongs to a different branch\").into())\n702\t    }\n703\t}\n704\t\n705\tasync fn ensure_work_order_branch_tx(\n706\t    tx: &mut Transaction<'_, QueryBuilder::<Postgres>::new(\n769\t        r#\"\n770\t        SELECT t.id, t.kind, t.branch_id, t.work_order_id, t.title,\n771\t               t.created_at, t.updated_at,\n772\t               lm.id AS last_message_id,\n773\t               lm.sent_at AS last_message_at,\n774\t               COUNT(tm_all.user_id)::BIGINT AS member_count\n775\t        FROM messenger_threads t\n776\t        LEFT        updated_at: row.try_get(\"updated_at\")?,\n929\t    })\n930\t}\n931\t\n932\tfn push_scope_filter(\n933\t    builder: &mut QueryBuilder<Postgres>,\n934\t    column: &str,\n935\t    scope: &BranchScope,\n936\t) -> Result<(), PgMessengerError> {\n937\t    match scope {\n938\t        BranchScope::All => Ok(()),\n939\t        BranchScope::Branches(branches) if branches.is_empty() => {\n940\t            builder.push(\" AND false\");\n941\t            Ok(())\n942\t        }\n943\t        BranchScope::Branches(branches) => {\n944\t            let branch_ids: Vec<uuid::Uuid> =\n945\t                branches.iter().map(|branch| *branch.as_uuid()).collect();\n946\t            builder.push(\" AND \");\n947\t            builder.push(column);\n948\t            builder.push(\" = ANY(\");\n949\t            builder.push_bind(branch_ids);\n950\t            builder.push(\")\");\n951\t            Ok(())\n952\t        }\n953\t    }\n954\t}\n955\t\n956\tfn Self::Db(DbError::Sqlx(sqlx::Error::RowNotFound)) => ErrorKind::NotFound,\n            Self::Db(DbError::Sqlx(sqlx::Error::Database(err)))\n                if err.code().is_some_and(|code| code == \"23505\") =>\n            {\n                ErrorKind::Conflict\n            }\n            Self::Db(_) => ErrorKind::Internal,\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nimpl From<sqlx::Error> for PgMessengerError command: CreateThreadCommand,\n    ) -> Result<ThreadSummary, PgMessengerError> {\n        ensure_branch_scope(&command.branch_scope, command.branch_id)?;\n        validate_thread_shape(&command)?;\n        let member_ids = normalized_members(command.actor, &command.member_ids)?;\n        let thread_id = ThreadId::new();\n        let branch_id = command.branch_id;\n        let org = current_org().map_err(KernelError::from)?;\n        let org_uuid = *org.as_uuid();\n        let event = messenger_audit_event(\n            \"message_thread.create\",\n            command.actor,\n            branch_id,\n            \"message_thread\",\n            thread_id,\n            command.trace,\n            command.occurred_at,\n        )?\n        .with_org(org);\n\n        with_audit::<_, ThreadSummary, PgMessengerError>(&self.pool, event, |tx| {\n            Box::pin(async move {\n                if let Some(work_order_id) = command.work_order_id {\n   id: thread_id,\n                        kind: command.kind,\n                        branch_id,\n                        work_order_id: command.work_order_id,\n                        title: }\n\n    pub async fn ensure_work_order_thread(\n        &self,\n        command: EnsureWorkOrderThreadCommand,\n    ) -> Result<ThreadSummary, PgMessengerError> {\n        if let Some(existing) =\n            fetch_work_order_thread_pool(&self.pool, command.work_order_id).await?\n        {\n            return Ok(existing);\n        }\n\n        let request_no = work_order_request_no(&self.pool, command.work_order_id).await?;\n        ensure_work_order_branch_pool(&self.pool, command.work_order_id, command.branch_id).await?;\n        let thread_id = ThreadId::new();\n        let org =        command.branch_id,\n            \"message_thread\",\n            thread_id,\n            command.trace,\n            command.occurred_at,\n        )?\n        .with_org(org);\n        let title KernelError::conflict(\"work-order messenger thread create raced\").into()\n                    })\n            }\n            Err(err) => Err(err),\n        }\n    }\n\n    pub async fn send_message(\n        &self,\n        command: SendMessageCommand,\n    ) -> Result<MessageSummary, PgMessengerError> {\n        let body = MessageBody::new(command.body)?;\n        let access = command.trace,\n            command.occurred_at,\n        )?\n        .with_org(org)\n        .with_snapshots(\n            None,\n            Some(serde_json::json!({\n                \"thread_id\":   .bind(sort_order)\n                    .bind(org_uuid)\n                    .execute(tx.as_mut())\n                    .await?;\n                }\n\n                sqlx::query(\"UPDATE messenger_threads SET updated_at = $2 WHERE id = $1\")\n                    .bind(*command.thread_id.as_uuid())\n                    .bind(command.occurred_at)\n                    .execute(tx.as_mut())\n                    .await?;\n\n                fetch_message_summary_tx(tx, message_id).await\n            })\n        })\n        .await?;\n\n        if let Some(notifier) =                 branch_id: summary.branch_id,\n                })\n                .await;\n        }\n\n        Ok(summary)\n    }\n\n    /// Coalesce read receipts at the thread/user level and audit one\n    /// `message.read` event per explicit read command rather than per message.\n    /// That preserves who acknowledged which latest message while avoiding an\n    /// audit row explosion for long catch-up pages.\n    pub async fn mark_thread_read(\n        &self,\n        command: MarkThreadReadCommand,\n    ) -> Result<ReadReceiptSummary, PgMessengerError> {\n        let access = command.thread_id,\n            command.trace,\n            command.occurred_at,\n        )?\n        .with_org(org)\n        .with_snapshots(\n            None,\n            Some(serde_json::json!({\n                \"last_read_message_id\": command.last_read_message_id,\n            })),\n        );\n\n        with_audit::<_, ReadReceiptSummary, PgMessengerError>(&self.pool, event, |tx| {\n            Box::pin(async move {\n                sqlx::query(\n                    r#\"\n                    INSERT INTO messenger_read_receipts (\n                        thread_id, user_id, last_read_message_id, read_at, updated_at, org_id\n                    )\n                    VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $4, $5)\n                    ON CONFLICT (thread_id, user_id) DO UPDATE\n                    SET last_read_message_id = EXCLUDED.last_read_message_id,\n                        read_at = EXCLUDED.read_at,\n                        updated_at = EXCLUDED.updated_at\n                    \"#,\n                )\n                .bind(*command.thread_id.as_uuid())\n                .bind(*command.actor.as_uuid())\n                .bind(*command.last_read_message_id.as_uuid())\n                .bind(command.occurred_at)\n                .bind(org_uuid)\n                .execute(tx.as_mut())\n                .await?;\n                fetch_read_receipt_tx(tx, command.thread_id, command.actor).await\n            })\n        })\n        .await\n    }\n\n    pub async fn list_threads(\n        &self,\n        query: ListThreadsQuery,\n    ) -> Result<Vec<ThreadSummary>, PgMessengerError> {\n        let limit = normalized_limit(query.limit);\n        let mut builder = QueryBuilder::<Postgres>::new(\n            r#\"\n            SELECT t.id, t.kind, t.branch_id, t.work_order_id, t.title,\n                   t.created_at, t.updated_at,\n                   lm.id AS last_message_id,\n                   lm.sent_at AS last_message_at,\n                   COUNT(tm_all.user_id)::BIGINT AS member_count\n            FROM messenger_threads t\n            JOIN messenger_thread_members tm_actor\n              ON tm_actor.thread_id = t.id\n             AND tm_actor.user_id =\n            \"#,\n        );\n        builder.push_bind(*query.actor.as_uuid());\n        builder.push(\n            r#\"\n            LEFT JOIN LATERAL (\n                SELECT id, sent_at\n                FROM messenger_messages\n                WHERE thread_id = t.id\n                ORDER BY sent_at DESC, id DESC\n                LIMIT 1\n            ) lm ON true\n            LEFT JOIN messenger_thread_members tm_all ON tm_all.thread_id = t.id\n            WHERE true\n            \"#,\n        );\n        push_scope_filter(&mut builder, \"t.branch_id\", &query.branch_scope)?;\n        builder.push(\n            r#\"\n            GROUP BY t.id, lm.id, lm.sent_at\n            ORDER BY COALESCE(lm.sent_at, t.updated_at) DESC, t.id DESC\n            LIMIT\n            \"#,\n        );\n        builder.push_bind(limit);\n\n        let org = current_org().map_err(KernelError::from)?;\n        let rows = with_org_conn::<_, _, PgMessengerError>(&self.pool, org, move |tx| {\n            Box::pin(async move { Ok(builder.build().fetch_all(tx.as_mut()).await?) })\n        })\n        .await?;\n        rows.iter().map(thread_summary_from_row).collect()\n    }\n\n    pub async fn message_page(\n        &self,\n        query: MessagePageQuery,\n    ) -> Result<MessagePage, PgMessengerError> {\n        require_thread_access(\n            &self.pool,\n            query.thread_id,\n            query.actor,\n            &query.branch_scope,\n        )\n        .await?;\n        let limit = normalized_limit(query.limit);\n        let page_limit = limit + 1;\n        let before = match query.before_message_id {\n            Some(message_id) => {\n                Some(message_cursor(&self.pool, message_id, query.thread_id).await?)\n            }\n            None => None,\n        };\n\n        let mut builder = message_select_builder();\n        builder.push(\" WHERE m.thread_id = \");\n        builder.push_bind(*query.thread_id.as_uuid());\n        if let Some((sent_at, id)) = before {\n            builder.push(\" AND (m.sent_at, m.id) < (\");\n            builder.push_bind(sent_at);\n            builder.push(\", \");\n            builder.push_bind(id);\n            builder.push(\")\");\n        }\n        builder.push(\" GROUP BY m.id, sender.display_name ORDER BY m.sent_at DESC, m.id DESC LIMIT \");\n        builder.push_bind(page_limit);\n\n        let org = current_org().map_err(KernelError::from)?;\n        let rows = with_org_conn::<_, _, PgMessengerError>(&self.pool, org, move |tx| {\n            Box::pin(async move { Ok(builder.build().fetch_all(tx.as_mut()).await?) })\n        })\n        .await?;\n        let mut items: Vec<MessageSummary> = rows\n            .iter()\n            .map(message_summary_from_row)\n            .collect::<Result<_, _>>()?;\n        let has_more = i64::try_from(items.len()).unwrap_or(0) > limit;\n        if has_more {\n            let _ = items.pop();\n        }\n        let next_cursor = if has_more {\n            items.last().map(|message| message.id)\n        } else {\n            None\n        };\n\n        Ok(MessagePage { items, next_cursor })\n    }\n\n    /// Search primarily uses the `search_vector` GIN index. PostgreSQL's\n    /// built-in `simple` configuration has limited Korean tokenization without\n    /// a mecab-style dictionary, so this T3.1 slice also applies an `ILIKE`\n    /// substring fallback for Korean terms. That keeps polling search useful\n    /// without pretending the FTS stack is linguistically complete.\n    pub async fn search_messages(\n        &self,\n        query: SearchMessagesQuery,\n    ) -> Result<Vec<MessageSummary>, PgMessengerError> {\n        let search = query.query.trim();\n        if search.is_empty() {\n            return Err(KernelError::validation(\"search query is required\").into());\n        }\n        let limit = normalized_limit(query.limit);\n        let mut builder = message_select_builder();\n        builder.push(\n            r#\"\n            JOIN messenger_thread_members tm_actor\n              ON tm_actor.thread_id = m.thread_id\n             AND tm_actor.user_id =\n            \"#,\n        );\n        builder.push_bind(*query.actor.as_uuid());\n        builder.push(\" WHERE (m.search_vector @@ plainto_tsquery('simple', \");\n        builder.push_bind(search);\n        builder.push(\") OR m.body ILIKE \");\n        builder.push_bind(format!(\"%{search}%\"));\n        builder.push(\")\");\n        push_scope_filter(&mut builder, \"m.branch_id\", &query.branch_scope)?;\n        builder.push(\" GROUP BY m.id, sender.display_name ORDER BY m.sent_at DESC, m.id DESC LIMIT \");\n        builder.push_bind(limit);\n\n        let org = current_org().map_err(KernelError::from)?;\n        let rows = with_org_conn::<_, _, PgMessengerError>(&self.pool, org, move |tx| {\n            Box::pin(async move { Ok(builder.build().fetch_all(tx.as_mut()).await?) })\n        })\n        .await?;\n        rows.iter().map(message_summary_from_row).collect()\n    }\n}\n\nimpl WorkOrderCreatedListener for PgMessengerStore {\n    fn work_order_created(&self, event: WorkOrderCreatedEvent) -> WorkOrderCreatedFuture<'_> {\n        Box::pin(async move {\n            self.ensure_work_order_thread(EnsureWorkOrderThreadCommand {\n                actor: event.actor,\n                branch_id: event.branch_id,\n                work_order_id: event.work_order_id,\n                trace: event.trace,\n                occurred_at: event.occurred_at,\n            })\n            .await\n            .map(|_| ())\n            .map_err(kernel_error_from_messenger_error)\n        })\n    }\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy)]\nstruct ThreadAccess {\n    branch_id: BranchId,\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy)]\nstruct NewThread<'a> {\n    id: ThreadId,\n    kind: ThreadKind,\n    branch_id: BranchId,\n    work_order_id: Option<WorkOrderId>,\n    title: Option<&'a str>,\n    actor: UserId,\n    occurred_at: time::OffsetDateTime,\n}\n\nfn validate_thread_shape(command: &CreateThreadCommand) -> Result<(), PgMessengerError> {\n    match command.kind {\n        ThreadKind::WorkOrder if command.work_order_id.is_none() => Err(KernelError::validation(\n            \"work-order messenger thread requires work_order_id\",\n        )\n        .into()),\n        ThreadKind::WorkOrder => Ok(()),\n        ThreadKind::Team | ThreadKind::Dm | ThreadKind::Group\n            if command.work_order_id.is_some() =>\n        {\n            Err(KernelError::validation(\n                \"only work-order messenger threads may carry work_order_id\",\n            )\n            .into())\n        }\n        ThreadKind::Dm if normalized_members(command.actor, &command.member_ids)?.len() != 2 => {\n            Err(KernelError::validation(\"DM thread requires exactly two members\").into())\n        }\n        ThreadKind::Group if normalized_members(command.actor, &command.member_ids)?.len() < 3 => {\n            Err(KernelError::validation(\"group thread requires at least three members\").into())\n        }\n        _ => Ok(()),\n    }\n}\n\nfn normalized_members(actor: UserId, members: &[UserId]) -> Result<Vec<UserId>, PgMessengerError> {\n    let mut members = members.to_vec();\n    members.push(actor);\n    members.sort();\n    members.dedup();\n    if members.is_empty() {\n        return Err(KernelError::validation(\"messenger thread requires members\").into());\n    }\n    Ok(members)\n}\n\nfn ensure_branch_scope(scope: &BranchScope, branch_id: BranchId) -> Result<(), PgMessengerError> {\n    if scope.allows(branch_id) {\n        Ok(())\n    } else {\n        Err(KernelError::forbidden(\"messenger branch is outside principal scope\").into())\n    }\n}\n\nfn normalized_limit(limit: i64) -> i64 {\n    limit.clamp(1, 100)\n}\n\nasync fn insert_thread_tx(\n    tx: &mut Transaction<'_, Postgres>,\n    thread: NewThread<'_>,\n    member_ids: &[UserId],\n    org_uuid: uuid::Uuid,\n) -> Result<(), PgMessengerError> {\n    sqlx::query(\n        r#\"\n        INSERT INTO messenger_threads (\n            id, kind, branch_id, work_order_id, title, created_by, created_at, updated_at, org_id\n        )\n        VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6, $7, $7, $8)\n        \"#,\n    )\n    .bind(*thread.id.as_uuid())\n    .bind(thread.kind.as_db_str())\n    .bind(*thread.branch_id.as_uuid())\n    .bind(thread.work_order_id.map(|id| *id.as_uuid()))\n    .bind(thread.title)\n    .bind(*thread.actor.as_uuid())\n    .bind(thread.occurred_at)\n    .bind(org_uuid)\n    .execute(tx.as_mut())\n    .await?;\n\n    for member_id in member_ids {\n        let role = if *member_id == thread.actor {\n            \"OWNER\"\n        } else {\n            \"MEMBER\"\n        };\n        sqlx::query(\n            r#\"\n            INSERT INTO messenger_thread_members (thread_id, user_id, role, joined_at, org_id)\n            VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5)\n            ON CONFLICT (thread_id, user_id) DO NOTHING\n            \"#,\n        )\n        .bind(*thread.id.as_uuid())\n        .bind(*member_id.as_uuid())\n        .bind(role)\n        .bind(thread.occurred_at)\n        .bind(org_uuid)\n        .execute(tx.as_mut())\n        .await?;\n    }\n\n    Ok(())\n}\n\nasync fn require_thread_access(\n    pool: &PgPool,\n    thread_id: ThreadId,\n    actor: UserId,\n    branch_scope: &BranchScope,\n) -> Result<ThreadAccess, PgMessengerError> {\n    let org = current_org().map_err(KernelError::from)?;\n    let row = with_org_conn::<_, _, PgMessengerError>(pool, org, move |tx| {\n        Box::pin(async move {\n            Ok(sqlx::query(\n                r#\"\n        SELECT t.branch_id,\n               EXISTS (\n                   SELECT 1\n                   FROM messenger_thread_members tm\n                   WHERE tm.thread_id = t.id\n                     AND tm.user_id = $2\n               ) AS is_member\n        FROM messenger_threads t\n        WHERE t.id = $1\n        \"#,\n            )\n            .bind(*thread_id.as_uuid())\n            .bind(*actor.as_uuid())\n            .fetch_optional(tx.as_mut())\n            .await?)\n        })\n    })\n    .await?\n    .ok_or_else(|| KernelError::not_found(\"messenger thread was not found\"))?;\n\n    let branch_id = .unwrap_or(false);\n    if !is_member {\n        return Err(KernelError::forbidden(\"actor is not a messenger thread member\").into());\n    }\n    Ok(ThreadAccess { branch_id })\n}\n\nasync fn )\n}\n\nfn thread_summary_from_row(row: &sqlx::postgres::PgRow) -> Result<ThreadSummary, PgMessengerError> {\n    let kind: String = row.try_get(\"kind\")?;\n    Ok(ThreadSummary {\n        id: QueryBuilder<Postgres> {\n    QueryBuilder::<Postgres>::new(\n        r#\"\n        SELECT m.id, m.thread_id, m.branch_id, m.sender_id, m.body,\n               m.sent_at, m.created_at, sender.display_name AS sender_name,\n               COALESCE(\n                   array_agg(a.evidence_id ORDER BY a.sort_order)\n                       FILTER (WHERE a.evidence_id IS NOT NULL),\n                   ARRAY[]::uuid[]\n               ) AS attachment_evidence_ids\n        FROM messenger_messages m\n        LEFT JOIN messenger_message_attachments a ON a.message_id = m.id\n        -- Same-org JOIN: `users` is RLS-scoped to app.current_org just like\n        -- messenger_messages, so this can only resolve a sender in the caller's\n        -- tenant. A cross-tenant or hard-deleted sender simply yields NULL.\n        LEFT JOIN users sender ON sender.id = m.sender_id\n        \"#,\n    )\n}\n\nasync fn fetch_message_summary_tx(\n    tx: &mut updated_at: row.try_get(\"updated_at\")?,\n    })\n}\n\nfn push_scope_filter(\n    builder: &mut QueryBuilder<Postgres>,\n    column: &str,\n    scope: &BranchScope,\n) -> Result<(), PgMessengerError> {\n    match scope {\n        BranchScope::All => Ok(()),\n        BranchScope::Branches(branches) if branches.is_empty() => {\n            builder.push(\" AND false\");\n            Ok(())\n        }\n        BranchScope::Branches(branches) => {\n            let branch_ids: Vec<uuid::Uuid> =\n                branches.iter().map(|branch| *branch.as_uuid()).collect();\n            builder.push(\" AND \");\n            builder.push(column);\n            builder.push(\" = ANY(\");\n            builder.push_bind(branch_ids);\n            builder.push(\")\");\n            Ok(())\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn kernel_error_from_messenger_error(err: PgMessengerError) -> KernelError {\n    match err {\n        PgMessengerError::Domain(err) => err,\n        PgMessengerError::Db(err) => KernelError::new(\n            ErrorKind::Internal,\n            format!(\"messenger store failed: {err}\"),\n        ),\n The caller then redeems the emailed code via\n/// `/auth/otp/redeem` and enrolls a passkey, reusing the existing flow unchanged.\nasync fn signup(\n    State(state): State<AuthRestState>,\n    headers: HeaderMap,\n    Json(body): Json<SignupRequest>,\n) -> Result<Response, RestError> {\n    let services = state.services()?;\n    let now = OffsetDateTime::now_utc();\n    rate_limit(\n        &state.pool,\n        &headers,\n        state.trusted_proxy_count,\n        RateLimitEndpoint::Signup,\n        now,\n    )\n    .await?;\n\n    let email = body.email.trim();\n    let display_name = signup_display_name(email)?;\n    let ttl = DEFAULT_SIGNUP_OTP_TTL;\n\n    let issue = services\n        .bootstrap_credentials\n        .signup_open_member(&state.pool, &display_name, now, ttl)\n        .await\n        .map_err(RestError::from_provisioning)?;\n\n    // Deliver the code out-of-band.
