Realtime is a background\n43\t    /// LISTEN/NOTIFY task with NO request context, so `current_org()` is not\n44\t    /// available in the listener; the publisher carries the org here so the\n45\t    /// listener can arm `app.current_org` before reading FORCE-RLS tables.\n46\t    pub org_id: OrgId,\n47\t}\n48\t\n49\timpl MessageNotifyPayload {\n50\t    #[must_use]\n51\t    pub fn from_notification(notification: MessagePostedNotification, org_id: OrgId) -> Self {\n52\t        Self {\n53\t            message_id: notification.message_id,\n54\t            thread_id: notification.thread_id,\n55\t            org_id,\n56\t        }\n57\t    }\n58\t\n59\t    pub fn to_json_bytes(&self) -> Result<Vec<u8>, NotifyPayloadError> {\n60\t        let bytes = serde_json::to_vec(self)?;\n61\t        validate_payload_size(&bytes)?;\n62\t        Ok(bytes)\n63\t    }\n64\t\n65\t    pub fn from_json_bytes(bytes: &[u8]) -> Result<Self, NotifyPayloadError> {\n66\t        validate_payload_size(bytes)?;\n67\t        Ok(serde_json::from_slice(bytes)?)\n68\t    }\n69\t}\n70\t\n71\t#[derive(Debug, thiserror::Error)]\n72\tpub enum NotifyPayloadError {\n73\t    #[error(\"NOTIFY payload is {size} bytes; it must be below {limit} bytes\")]\n74\t    PayloadTooLarge { size: usize, limit: usize },\n75\t\n76\t    #[error(transparent)]\n77\t    Serialize(#[from] serde_json::Error),\n78\t\n79\t    #[error(transparent)]\n80\t    Database(#[from] sqlx::Error),\n81\t\n82\t    #[error(transparent)]\n83\t    RequestContext(#[from] RequestContextError),\n84\t}\n85\t\n86\t#[derive(Debug, thiserror::Error)]\n87\tpub enum RealtimeError {\n88\t    #[error(\"database is not configured for realtime\")]\n89\t    DatabaseNotConfigured,\n90\t\n91\t    #[error(transparent)]\n92\t    Database(#[from] sqlx::Error),\n93\t\n94\t    #[error(transparent)]\n95\t    NotifyPayload(#[from] NotifyPayloadError),\n96\t\n97\t    #[error(transparent)]\n98\t    Db(#[from] DbError),\n99\t\n100\t    #[error(transparent)]\n101\t    RequestContext(#[from] RequestContextError),\n102\t\n103\t    #[error(\"realtime connection closed during replay\")]\n104\t    ConnectionClosed,\n105\t\n106\t    #[error(\"realtime replay consumer did not drain within {timeout:?}\")]\n107\t    ReplayTimedOut { timeout: Duration },\n108\t}\n109\t\n110\t#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\n111\tpub struct PostgresMessageNotifier {\n112\t    pool: PgPool,\n113\t}\n114\t\n115\timpl PostgresMessageNotifier {\n116\t    #[must_use]\n117\t    pub fn new(pool: PgPool) -> Self {\n118\t        Self { pool }\n119\t    }\n120\t\n121\t    pub async fn notify_message_posted(\n122\t        &self,\n123\t        notification: MessagePostedNotification,\n124\t    ) -> Result<(), NotifyPayloadError> {\n125\t        // The publisher runs inside the message-send request task, where the\n126\t        // tenant is armed, so `current_org()` resolves the org to stamp onto the\n127\t        // payload. The background listener has no request context and reads it\n128\t        // back to arm `app.current_org` before any FORCE-RLS table read.\n129\t        let org = current_org()?;\n130\t        let payload = MessageNotifyPayload::from_notification(notification, org).to_json_bytes()?;\n131\t        Self::validate_payload_size_for_test(&payload)?;\n132\t        let payload = String::from_utf8(payload).map_err(|err| {\n133\t            serde_json::Error::io(std::io::Error::new(std::io::ErrorKind::InvalidData, err))\n134\t        })?;\n135\t\n136\t        sqlx::query(\"SELECT pg_notify($1, $2)\")\n137\t            .bind(MESSAGE_POSTED_CHANNEL)\n138\t            .bind(payload)\n139\t            // rls-arming: ok pg_notify is not a tenant-table read\n140\t            .execute(&self.pool)\n141\t            .await?;\n142\t        Ok(())\n143\t    }\n144\t\n145\t    pub fn validate_payload_size_for_test(bytes: &[u8]) -> Result<(), NotifyPayloadError> {\n146\t        validate_payload_size(bytes)\n147\t    }\n148\t}\n149\t\n150\timpl MessageNotifier for PostgresMessageNotifier {\n151\t    fn message_posted(&self, notification: MessagePostedNotification) -> MessageNotifyFuture<'_> {\n152\t        Box::pin(async move {\n153\t            if let Err(err) = self.notify_message_posted(notification).await {\n154\t                tracing::error!(error = %err, \"failed to publish messenger realtime notification\");\n155\t            }\n156\t        })\n157\t    }\n158\t}\n159\t\n160\tfn validate_payload_size(bytes: &[u8]) -> Result<(), NotifyPayloadError> {\n161\t    if bytes.len() >= NOTIFY_PAYLOAD_LIMIT_BYTES {\n162\t        Err(NotifyPayloadError::PayloadTooLarge {\n163\t            size: bytes.len(),\n164\t            limit: NOTIFY_PAYLOAD_LIMIT_BYTES,\n165\t        })\n166\t    } else {\n167\t        Ok(())\n168\t    }\n169\t}\n170\t\n171\t#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Serialize, Deserialize)]\n172\t#[serde(tag = \"type\", rename_all = \"snake_case\")]\n173\tpub enum RealtimeEvent {\n174\t    MessagePosted { message: MessageSummary },\n175\t}\n176\t\n177\timpl RealtimeEvent {\n178\t    fn message_id(&self) -> MessageId {\n179\t        match self {\n180\t            Self::MessagePosted { message } => message.id,\n181\t        }\n182\t    }\n183\t\n184\t    fn cursor(&self) -> MessageCursor {\n185\t        match self {\n186\t            Self::MessagePosted { message } => MessageCursor {\n187\t                sent_at: message.sent_at,\n188\t                id: message.id,\n189\t            },\n190\t        }\n191\t    }\n192\t\n193\t    fn branch_id(&self) -> BranchId {\n194\t        match self {\n195\t            Self::MessagePosted { message } => message.branch_id,\n196\t        }\n197\t    }\n198\t\n199\t    fn thread_id(&self) -> ThreadId {\n200\t        match self {\n201\t            Self::MessagePosted { message } => message.thread_id,\n202\t        }\n203\t    }\n204\t}\n205\t\n206\t#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, PartialOrd, Ord)]\n207\tstruct MessageCursor {\n208\t    sent_at: time::OffsetDateTime,\n209\t    id: MessageId,\n210\t}\n211\t\n212\t#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq)]\n213\tpub struct RealtimeHubConfig {\n214\t    pub connection_buffer: usize,\n215\t}\n216\t\n217\timpl Default for RealtimeHubConfig {\n218\t    fn default() -> Self {\n219\t        Self {\n220\t            connection_buffer: DEFAULT_CONNECTION_BUFFER,\n221\t        }\n222\t    }\n223\t}\n224\t\n225\t#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq)]\n226\tpub struct RealtimePrincipal {\n227\t    pub user_id: UserId,\n228\t    pub branch_scope: BranchScope,\n229\t    /// The subscriber's tenant, taken from the authenticated WS session's JWT\n230\t    /// `org` claim. Replay reads run in a background task with no request\n231\t    /// context, so this org arms `app.current_org` for the subscriber's own\n232\t    /// FORCE-RLS reads.\n233\t    pub org_id: OrgId,\n234\t}\n235\t\n236\t#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Serialize, Deserialize)]\n237\t#[serde(rename_all = \"snake_case\")]\n238\tpub enum DisconnectReason {\n239\t    LaggingConsumer,\n240\t    ReplayFailed,\n241\t    ServerShutdown,\n242\t}\n243\t\n244\t#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Serialize, Deserialize)]\n245\tpub struct DisconnectNotice {\n246\t    pub reason: DisconnectReason,\n247\t    pub resume_after: Option<MessageId>,\n248\t}\n249\t\n250\t#[derive(Debug)]\n251\tpub struct RealtimeConnection {\n252\t    id: uuid::Uuid,\n253\t    events_rx: mpsc::Receiver<RealtimeEvent>,\n254\t    disconnect_rx: mpsc::UnboundedReceiver<DisconnectNotice>,\n255\t}\n256\t\n257\timpl RealtimeConnection {\n258\t    #[must_use]\n259\t    pub fn id(&self) -> uuid::Uuid {\n260\t        self.id\n261\t    }\n262\t\n263\t    pub async fn recv(&mut self) -> Option<RealtimeEvent> {\n264\t        self.events_rx.recv().await\n265\t    }\n266\t\n267\t    pub async fn disconnect(&mut self) -> Option<DisconnectNotice> {\n268\t        self.disconnect_rx.recv().await\n269\t    }\n270\t\n271\t    fn into_parts(\n272\t        self,\n273\t    ) -> (\n274\t        uuid::Uuid,\n275\t        mpsc::Receiver<RealtimeEvent>,\n276\t        mpsc::UnboundedReceiver<DisconnectNotice>,\n277\t    ) {\n278\t        (self.id, self.events_rx, self.disconnect_rx)\n279\t    }\n280\t}\n281\t\n282\t#[derive(Debug)]\n283\tstruct ConnectionSlot {\n284\t    principal: RealtimePrincipal,\n285\t    events_tx: mpsc::Sender<RealtimeEvent>,\n286\t    disconnect_tx: mpsc::UnboundedSender<DisconnectNotice>,\n287\t    delivery_state: ConnectionDeliveryState,\n288\t}\n289\t\n290\t#[derive(Debug)]\n291\tenum ConnectionDeliveryState {\n292\t    Live,\n293\t    Replaying {\n294\t        buffered_events: Vec<RealtimeEvent>,\n295\t        replay_cursor: Option<MessageCursor>,\n296\t    },\n297\t}\n298\t\n299\t#[derive(Debug)]\n300\tpub struct PgRealtimeHub {\n301\t    pool: Option<PgPool>,\n302\t    config: RealtimeHubConfig,\n303\t    connections: Mutex<HashMap<uuid::Uuid, ConnectionSlot>>,\n304\t}\n305\t\n306\timpl PgRealtimeHub {\n307\t    #[must_use]\n308\t    pub fn new(pool: PgPool, config: RealtimeHubConfig) -> Self {\n309\t        Self {\n310\t            pool: Some(pool),\n311\t            config,\n312\t            connections: Mutex::new(HashMap::new()),\n313\t        }\n314\t    }\n315\t\n316\t    #[must_use]\n317\t    pub fn for_tests(config: RealtimeHubConfig) -> Self {\n318\t        Self {\n319\t            pool: None,\n320\t            config,\n321\t            connections: Mutex::new(HashMap::new()),\n322\t        }\n323\t    }\n324\t\n325\t    pub async fn connect(\n326\t        self: &Arc<Self>,\n327\t        principal: RealtimePrincipal,\n328\t        last_message_id: Option<MessageId>,\n329\t    ) -> Result<RealtimeConnection, RealtimeError> {\n330\t        if last_message_id.is_some() && self.pool.is_none() {\n331\t            return Err(RealtimeError::DatabaseNotConfigured);\n332\t        }\n333\t\n334\t        let capacity = self.config.connection_buffer.max(1);\n335\t        let (events_tx, events_rx) = mpsc::channel(capacity);\n336\t        let (disconnect_tx, disconnect_rx) = mpsc::unbounded_channel();\n337\t        let id = uuid::Uuid::new_v4();\n338\t        let delivery_state = if last_message_id.is_some() {\n339\t            ConnectionDeliveryState::Replaying {\n340\t                buffered_events: Vec::new(),\n341\t                replay_cursor: None,\n342\t            }\n343\t        } else {\n344\t            ConnectionDeliveryState::Live\n345\t        };\n346\t        self.connections.lock().await.insert(\n347\t            id,\n348\t            ConnectionSlot {\n349\t                principal: principal.clone(),\n350\t                events_tx,\n351\t                disconnect_tx,\n352\t                delivery_state,\n353\t            },\n354\t        );\n355\t\n356\t        if let Some(last_message_id) = last_message_id {\n357\t            let hub = Arc::clone(self);\n358\t            tokio::spawn(async move {\n359\t                hub.run_replay(id, principal, last_message_id).await;\n360\t            });\n361\t        }\n362\t\n363\t        Ok(RealtimeConnection {\n364\t            id,\n365\t            events_rx,\n366\t            disconnect_rx,\n367\t        })\n368\t    }\n369\t\n370\t    pub async fn connection_count(&self) -> usize {\n371\t        self.connections.lock().await.len()\n372\t    }\n373\t\n374\t    pub async fn remove_connection(&self, connection_id: uuid::Uuid) {\n375\t        self.connections.lock().await.remove(&connection_id);\n376\t    }\n377\t\n378\t    pub async fn dispatch_local_for_test(\n379\t        &self,\n380\t        org: OrgId,\n381\t        event: RealtimeEvent,\n382\t    ) -> Result<(), RealtimeError> {\n383\t        self.dispatch_event(org, event, None).await\n384\t    }\n385\t\n386\t    pub async fn shutdown(&self) {\n387\t        let mut connections = self.connections.lock().await;\n388\t        for (_, slot) in connections.drain() {\n389\t            let _ = slot.disconnect_tx.send(DisconnectNotice {\n390\t                reason: DisconnectReason::ServerShutdown,\n391\t                resume_after: None,\n392\t            });\n393\t        }\n394\t    }\n395\t\n396\t    pub async fn start_postgres_listener(\n397\t        self: Arc<Self>,\n398\t    ) -> Result<PostgresBridgeHandle, RealtimeError> {\n399\t        let pool = self\n400\t            .pool\n401\t            .as_ref()\n402\t            .ok_or(RealtimeError::DatabaseNotConfigured)?\n403\t            .clone();\n404\t        let mut listener = PgListener::connect_with(&pool).await?;\n405\t        listener.listen(MESSAGE_POSTED_CHANNEL).await?;\n406\t        let (shutdown_tx, mut shutdown_rx) = watch::channel(false);\n407\t        let hub = Arc::clone(&self);\n408\t\n409\t        tokio::spawn(async move {\n410\t            loop {\n411\t                tokio::select! {\n412\t                    changed = shutdown_rx.changed() => {\n413\t                        if changed.is_err() || *shutdown_rx.borrow() {\n414\t                            break;\n415\t                        }\n416\t                    }\n417\t                    notification = listener.recv() => {\n418\t                        match notification {\n419\t                            Ok(notification) => {\n420\t                                if notification.channel() == MESSAGE_POSTED_CHANNEL\n421\t                                    && let Err(err) = hub.handle_notify_payload(notification.payload()).await\n422\t                                {\n423\t                                    tracing::warn!(error = %err, \"failed to handle messenger realtime notification\");\n424\t                                }\n425\t                            }\n426\t                            Err(err) => {\n427\t                                tracing::warn!(error = %err, \"Postgres realtime listener failed; retrying\");\n428\t                                tokio::time::sleep(Duration::from_millis(100)).await;\n429\t                            }\n430\t                        }\n431\t                    }\n432\t                }\n433\t            }\n434\t        });\n435\t\n436\t        Ok(PostgresBridgeHandle { shutdown_tx })\n437\t    }\n438\t\n439\t    async fn handle_notify_payload(&self, payload: &str) -> Result<(), RealtimeError> {\n440\t        let payload = MessageNotifyPayload::from_json_bytes(payload.as_bytes())?;\n441\t        // The listener has no request context; the org rides on the payload and\n442\t        // scopes every FORCE-RLS read triggered by this notification.\n443\t        let org = payload.org_id;\n444\t        let message = self\n445\t            .fetch_message(org, payload.message_id, payload.thread_id)\n446\t            .await?;\n447\t        self.dispatch_event(org, RealtimeEvent::MessagePosted { message }, None)\n448\t            .await\n449\t    }\n450\t\n451\t    async fn run_replay(\n452\t        self: Arc<Self>,\n453\t        connection_id: uuid::Uuid,\n454\t        principal: RealtimePrincipal,\n455\t        last_message_id: MessageId,\n456\t    ) {\n457\t        let result = async {\n458\t            self.replay_after(connection_id, &principal, last_message_id)\n459\t                .await?;\n460\t            self.finish_replay(connection_id).await\n461\t        }\n462\t        .await;\n463\t\n464\t        if let Err(err) = result {\n465\t            tracing::warn!(error = %err, \"realtime replay failed\");\n466\t            let resume_after = self.replay_resume_after(connection_id).await;\n467\t            self.disconnect_connection(connection_id, DisconnectReason::ReplayFailed, resume_after)\n468\t                .await;\n469\t        }\n470\t    }\n471\t\n472\t    async fn replay_after(\n473\t        &self,\n474\t        connection_id: uuid::Uuid,\n475\t        principal: &RealtimePrincipal,\n476\t        last_message_id: MessageId,\n477\t    ) -> Result<(), RealtimeError> {\n478\t        let pool = self\n479\t            .pool\n480\t            .as_ref()\n481\t            .ok_or(RealtimeError::DatabaseNotConfigured)?;\n482\t        // Replay runs in a spawned task with no request context, so the org is\n483\t        // carried from the authenticated subscriber session (`principal.org_id`)\n484\t        // and arms `app.current_org` for every FORCE-RLS read below.\n485\t        let org = principal.org_id;\n486\t        let last_message_uuid = *last_message_id.as_uuid();\n487\t        let cursor_row = with_org_conn::<_, _, RealtimeError>(pool, org, move |tx| {\n488\t            Box::pin(async move {\n489\t                Ok(\n490\t                    sqlx::query(\"SELECT sent_at, id FROM messenger_messages WHERE id = $1\")\n491\t                        .bind(last_message_uuid)\n492\t                        .fetch_optional(tx.as_mut())\n493\t                        .await?,\n494\t                )\n495\t            })\n496\t        })\n497\t        .await?;\n498\t        let Some(cursor) = cursor_row else {\n499\t            return Ok(());\n500\t        };\n501\t        let mut cursor = MessageCursor {\n502\t            sent_at: cursor.try_get(\"sent_at\")?,\n503\t            id: MessageId::from_uuid(cursor.try_get(\"id\")?),\n504\t        };\n505\t\n506\t        loop {\n507\t            let cursor_sent_at = cursor.sent_at;\n508\t            let cursor_id = *cursor.id.as_uuid();\n509\t            let branch_scope = principal.branch_scope.clone();\n510\t            let user_uuid = *principal.user_id.as_uuid();\n511\t            let rows = with_org_conn::<_, _, RealtimeError>(pool, org, move |tx| {\n512\t                Box::pin(async move {\n513\t                    let mut builder = message_select_builder();\n514\t                    builder.push(\n515\t                        r#\"\n516\t                JOIN messenger_thread_members tm\n517\t                  ON tm.thread_id = m.thread_id\n518\t                 AND tm.user_id =\n519\t                \"#,\n520\t                    );\n521\t                    builder.push_bind(user_uuid);\n522\t                    builder.push(\" WHERE (m.sent_at, m.id) > (\");\n523\t                    builder.push_bind(cursor_sent_at);\n524\t                    builder.push(\", \");\n525\t                    builder.push_bind(cursor_id);\n526\t                    builder.push(\")\");\n527\t                    push_scope_filter(&mut builder, \"m.branch_id\", &branch_scope);\n528\t                    builder.push(\" GROUP BY m.id ORDER BY m.sent_at ASC, m.id ASC LIMIT \");\n529\t                    builder.push_bind(REPLAY_PAGE_SIZE);\n530\t                    Ok(builder.build().fetch_all(tx.as_mut()).await?)\n531\t                })\n532\t            })\n533\t            .await?;\n534\t            if rows.is_empty() {\n535\t                break;\n536\t            }\n537\t\n538\t            let row_count = rows.len();\n539\t            for row in rows {\n540\t                let message = message_summary_from_row(&row)?;\n541\t                cursor = MessageCursor {\n542\t                    sent_at: message.sent_at,\n543\t                    id: message.id,\n544\t                };\n545\t                let event = RealtimeEvent::MessagePosted { message };\n546\t                if !self.send_replay_event(connection_id, event).await? {\n547\t                    return Ok(());\n548\t                }\n549\t            }\n550\t\n551\t            if row_count < usize::try_from(REPLAY_PAGE_SIZE).unwrap_or(usize::MAX) {\n552\t                break;\n553\t            }\n554\t        }\n555\t        Ok(())\n556\t    }\n557\t\n558\t    async fn fetch_message(\n559\t        &self,\n560\t        org: OrgId,\n561\t        message_id: MessageId,\n562\t        thread_id: ThreadId,\n563\t    ) -> Result<MessageSummary, RealtimeError> {\n564\t        let pool = self\n565\t            .pool\n566\t            .as_ref()\n567\t            .ok_or(RealtimeError::DatabaseNotConfigured)?;\n568\t        let message_uuid = *message_id.as_uuid();\n569\t        let thread_uuid = *thread_id.as_uuid();\n570\t        // The org is carried from the NOTIFY payload; arm it so this read sees\n571\t        // the publishing tenant's FORCE-RLS rows.\n572\t        with_org_conn::<_, _, RealtimeError>(pool, org, move |tx| {\n573\t            Box::pin(async move {\n574\t                let mut builder = message_select_builder();\n575\t                builder.push(\" WHERE m.id = \");\n576\t                builder.push_bind(message_uuid);\n577\t                builder.push(\" AND m.thread_id = \");\n578\t                builder.push_bind(thread_uuid);\n579\t                builder.push(\" GROUP BY m.id\");\n580\t                let row = builder.build().fetch_one(tx.as_mut()).await?;\n581\t                message_summary_from_row(&row).map_err(|err| RealtimeError::Db(DbError::Sqlx(err)))\n582\t            })\n583\t        })\n584\t        .await\n585\t    }\n586\t\n587\t    async fn dispatch_event(\n588\t        &self,\n589\t        org: OrgId,\n590\t        event: RealtimeEvent,\n591\t        authorized_users: Option<HashSet<UserId>>,\n592\t    ) -> Result<(), RealtimeError> {\n593\t        let branch_id = event.branch_id();\n594\t        let candidate_users = if authorized_users.is_some() || self.pool.is_none() {\n595\t            authorized_users\n596\t        } else {\n597\t            let candidates = {\n598\t                let connections = self.connections.lock().await;\n599\t                connections\n600\t                    .values()\n601\t                    .filter(|slot| slot.principal.branch_scope.allows(branch_id))\n602\t                    .map(|slot| slot.principal.user_id)\n603\t                    .collect::<Vec<_>>()\n604\t            };\n605\t            Some(\n606\t                self.authorized_thread_members(org, event.thread_id(), candidates)\n607\t                    .await?,\n608\t            )\n609\t        };\n610\t\n611\t        let targets = {\n612\t            let connections = self.connections.lock().await;\n613\t            connections\n614\t                .iter()\n615\t                .filter(|(_, slot)| slot.principal.branch_scope.allows(branch_id))\n616\t                .filter(|(_, slot)| {\n617\t                    candidate_users\n618\t                        .as_ref()\n619\t                        .is_none_or(|users| users.contains(&slot.principal.user_id))\n620\t                })\n621\t                .map(|(id, _)| *id)\n622\t                .collect::<Vec<_>>()\n623\t        };\n624\t\n625\t        for }\n631\t\n632\t    async fn send_replay_event(\n633\t        &self,\n634\t        connection_id: uuid::Uuid,\n635\t        event: RealtimeEvent,\n636\t    ) -> Result<bool, RealtimeError> {\n637\t        let cursor = event.cursor();\n638\t        let events_tx = {\n639\t            let connections = self.connections.lock().await;\n640\t            let Some(slot) = connections.get(&connection_id) else {\n641\t                return Ok(false);\n642\t            };\n643\t            slot.events_tx.clone()\n644\t        };\n645\t\n646\t        match tokio::time::timeout(REPLAY_SEND_TIMEOUT, events_tx.send(event)).await {\n647\t            Ok(Ok(())) => {\n648\t                self.mark_replay_cursor(connection_id, cursor).await;\n649\t                Ok(true)\n650\t            }\n651\t            Ok(Err(_)) => {\n652\t                self.remove_connection(connection_id).await;\n653\t                Err(RealtimeError::ConnectionClosed)\n654\t            }\n655\t            Err(_) => {\n656\t                let resume_after = self.replay_resume_after(connection_id).await;\n657\t                self.disconnect_connection(\n658\t                    connection_id,\n659\t                    DisconnectReason::LaggingConsumer,\n660\t                    resume_after,\n661\t                )\n662\t                .await;\n663\t                Err(RealtimeError::ReplayTimedOut {\n664\t                    timeout: REPLAY_SEND_TIMEOUT,\n665\t                })\n666\t            }\n667\t        }\n668\t    }\n669\t\n670\t    async fn finish_replay(&self, connection_id: uuid::Uuid) -> Result<(), RealtimeError> {\n671\t        loop {\n672\t            let events = {\n673\t                let mut connections = self.connections.lock().await;\n674\t                let Some(slot) = connections.get_mut(&connection_id) else {\n675\t                    return Ok(());\n676\t                };\n677\t                match &mut slot.delivery_state {\n678\t                    ConnectionDeliveryState::Live => return Ok(()),\n679\t                    ConnectionDeliveryState::Replaying {\n680\t                        buffered_events,\n681\t                        replay_cursor,\n682\t                    } => {\n683\t                        if buffered_events.is_empty() {\n684\t                            slot.delivery_state = ConnectionDeliveryState::Live;\n685\t                            return Ok(());\n686\t                        }\n687\t                        let replay_cursor = *replay_cursor;\n688\t                        let mut events = std::mem::take(buffered_events);\n689\t                        events.sort_by_key(RealtimeEvent::cursor);\n690\t                        let mut seen = HashSet::new();\n691\t                        events.retain(|event| {\n692\t                            let cursor = event.cursor();\n693\t                            replay_cursor.is_none_or(|replay_cursor| cursor > replay_cursor)\n694\t                                && seen.insert(event.message_id())\n695\t                        });\n696\t                        events\n697\t                    }\n698\t                }\n699\t            };\n700\t\n701\t            for event in events {\n702\t                if !self.send_replay_event(connection_id, event).await? {\n703\t                    return Ok(());\n704\t                }\n705\t            }\n706\t        }\n707\t    }\n708\t\n709\t    async fn mark_replay_cursor(&self, connection_id: uuid::Uuid, cursor: MessageCursor) {\n710\t        let mut connections = self.connections.lock().await;\n711\t        if let Some(slot) = connections.get_mut(&connection_id)\n712\t            && let ConnectionDeliveryState::Replaying { replay_cursor, .. } =\n713\t                &mut slot.delivery_state\n714\t        {\n715\t            *replay_cursor = Some(cursor);\n716\t        }\n717\t    }\n718\t\n719\t    async fn replay_resume_after(&self, connection_id: uuid::Uuid) -> Option<MessageId> {\n720\t        let connections = self.connections.lock().await;\n721\t        connections\n722\t            .get(&connection_id)\n723\t            .and_then(|slot| match &slot.delivery_state {\n724\t                ConnectionDeliveryState::Live => None,\n725\t                ConnectionDeliveryState::Replaying { replay_cursor, .. } => {\n726\t                    replay_cursor.map(|cursor| cursor.id)\n727\t                }\n728\t            })\n729\t    }\n730\t\n731\t    async fn disconnect_connection(\n732\t        &self,\n733\t        connection_id: uuid::Uuid,\n734\t        reason: DisconnectReason,\n735\t        resume_after: Option<MessageId>,\n736\t    ) {\n737\t        let mut connections = self.connections.lock().await;\n738\t        if let Some(slot) = connections.remove(&connection_id) {\n739\t            let _ = slot.disconnect_tx.send(DisconnectNotice {\n740\t                reason,\n741\t                resume_after,\n742\t            });\n743\t        }\n744\t    }\n745\t\n746\t    async fn dispatch_to_connection(\n747\t        &self,\n748\t        connection_id: uuid::Uuid,\n749\t        event: RealtimeEvent,\n750\t        resume_after: Option<MessageId>,\n751\t    ) {\n752\t        let mut connections = self.connections.lock().await;\n753\t        let slot.delivery_state {\n759\t            ConnectionDeliveryState::Live => {\n760\t                if slot.events_tx.try_send(event).is_err() {\n761\t                    disconnect_resume_after = replay_cursor,\n767\t            } => {\n768\t                if buffered_events.len() >= self.config.connection_buffer.max(1) {\n769\t                    disconnect_resume_after =\n770\t                        Some(replay_cursor.map(|cursor| cursor.id).or(resume_after));\n771\t                } else {\n772\t                    buffered_events.push(event);\n773\t                }\n774\t            }\n775\t        }\n776\t\n777\t        if let Some(resume_after) = disconnect_resume_after\n778\t            && let Some(slot) = connections.remove(&connection_id)\n779\t        {\n780\t            let _ = slot.disconnect_tx.send(DisconnectNotice {\n781\t                reason: DisconnectReason::LaggingConsumer,\n782\t                resume_after,\n783\t            });\n784\t        }\n785\t    }\n786\t\n787\t    async fn authorized_thread_members(\n788\t        &self,\n789\t        org: OrgId,\n790\t        thread_id: ThreadId,\n791\t        candidates: Vec<UserId>,\n792\t    ) -> Result<HashSet<UserId>, RealtimeError> {\n793\t        let Some(pool) = &self.pool else {\n794\t            return Ok(candidates.into_iter().collect());\n795\t        };\n796\t        if offered subprotocol, so select `bearer` to\n879\t        // complete the handshake (without this the browser aborts with \"Sent\n880\t        // non-empty 'Sec-WebSocket-Protocol' header but no response was received\").\n881\t        .protocols([\"bearer\"])\n882\t        .on_upgrade(move |socket| {\n883\t            websocket_session(state, principal, query.last_message_id, socket)\n884\t        })\n885\t        .into_response())\n886\t}\n887\t\n888\tasync fn websocket_session(\n889\t    state: RealtimeRestState,\n890\t    principal: RealtimePrincipal,\n891\t    last_message_id:       Err(err) => {\n897\t            tracing::warn!(error = %err, \"realtime websocket connect failed\");\n898\t            let _ = socket\n899\t                .send(Message::Close(Some(CloseFrame    }\n906\t    };\n907\t    let (connection_id, mut events_rx, mut disconnect_rx) = connection.into_parts();\n908\t\n909\t    loop {\n910\t        tokio::select! {\n911\t            notice = PostgreSQL remains the source of truth. `LISTEN/NOTIFY` carries only IDs\n//! and wakes local WebSocket hubs so they can re-read messages before fan-out.\n#![cfg_attr(test, allow(clippy::unwrap_used, clippy::expect_used, clippy::panic))]\n\nuse std::collections::{HashMap, HashSet};\nuse std::str::FromStr;\nuse std::sync::Arc;\nuse std::time::Duration;\n\nuse axum::extract::ws::{CloseFrame, Message, WebSocket, WebSocketUpgrade};\nuse axum::extract::{Query, State};\nuse axum::http::{HeaderMap, StatusCode, header};\nuse axum::response::{IntoResponse, Response};\nuse axum::routing::get;\nuse axum::{Json, Router};\nuse mnt_kernel_core::{BranchId, BranchScope, MessageId, OrgId, ThreadId, UserId};\nuse mnt_messenger_application::{\n    MessageNotifier, MessageNotifyFuture, MessagePostedNotification, MessageSummary,\n};\nuse mnt_platform_auth::{AccessClaims, JwtVerifier};\nuse mnt_platform_db::{DbError, with_org_conn};\nuse mnt_platform_request_context::{RequestContextError, current_org};\nuse serde::{Deserialize, Serialize};\nuse sqlx::postgres::PgListener;\nuse sqlx::{PgPool, Postgres, QueryBuilder, Row};\nuse tokio::sync::{Mutex, mpsc, watch};\n\npub const MESSAGE_POSTED_CHANNEL: &str = \"message_posted\";\npub const NOTIFY_PAYLOAD_LIMIT_BYTES: usize = 8000;\npub const DEFAULT_CONNECTION_BUFFER: usize = 64;\npub const REPLAY_PAGE_SIZE: i64 = 100;\npub const REPLAY_SEND_TIMEOUT: Duration = Duration::from_secs(30);\npub const WS_ROUTE_PATHS: &[&str] = &[\"/api/v1/ws\"];\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Serialize, Deserialize)]\n#[serde(deny_unknown_fields)]\npub struct MessageNotifyPayload {\n    pub message_id: MessageId,\n    pub thread_id: ThreadId,\n    /// The tenant that owns the posted message. Realtime is a background\n    /// LISTEN/NOTIFY task with NO request context, so `current_org()` is not\n    /// available in the listener; the publisher carries the org here so the\n    /// listener can arm `app.current_org` before reading FORCE-RLS tables.\n    pub org_id: OrgId,\n}\n\nimpl MessageNotifyPayload {\n    #[must_use]\n    pub fn from_notification(notification: MessagePostedNotification, org_id: OrgId) -> Self {\n        Self {\n            message_id: notification.message_id,\n            thread_id: notification.thread_id,\n            org_id,\n        }\n    }\n\n    pub fn to_json_bytes(&self) -> Result<Vec<u8>, NotifyPayloadError> {\n        let bytes = serde_json::to_vec(self)?;\n        validate_payload_size(&bytes)?;\n        Ok(bytes)\n    }\n\n    pub fn from_json_bytes(bytes: &[u8]) -> Result<Self, NotifyPayloadError> {\n        validate_payload_size(bytes)?;\n        Ok(serde_json::from_slice(bytes)?)\n    }\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, thiserror::Error)]\npub enum NotifyPayloadError {\n    #[error(\"NOTIFY payload is {size} bytes; it must be below {limit} bytes\")]\n    PayloadTooLarge { size: usize, limit: usize },\n\n    #[error(transparent)]\n    Serialize(#[from] serde_json::Error),\n\n    #[error(transparent)]\n    Database(#[from] sqlx::Error),\n\n    #[error(transparent)]\n    RequestContext(#[from] RequestContextError),\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, thiserror::Error)]\npub enum RealtimeError {\n    #[error(\"database is not configured for realtime\")]\n    DatabaseNotConfigured,\n\n    #[error(transparent)]\n    Database(#[from] sqlx::Error),\n\n    #[error(transparent)]\n    NotifyPayload(#[from] NotifyPayloadError),\n\n    #[error(transparent)]\n    Db(#[from] DbError),\n\n    #[error(transparent)]\n    RequestContext(#[from] RequestContextError),\n\n    #[error(\"realtime connection closed during replay\")]\n    ConnectionClosed,\n\n    #[error(\"realtime replay consumer did not drain within {timeout:?}\")]\n    ReplayTimedOut { timeout: Duration },\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct PostgresMessageNotifier {\n    pool: PgPool,\n}\n\nimpl PostgresMessageNotifier {\n    #[must_use]\n    pub fn new(pool: PgPool) -> Self {\n        Self { pool }\n    }\n\n    pub async fn notify_message_posted(\n        &self,\n        notification: MessagePostedNotification,\n    ) -> Result<(), NotifyPayloadError> {\n        // The publisher runs inside the message-send request task, where the\n        // tenant is armed, so `current_org()` resolves the org to stamp onto the\n        // payload. The background listener has no request context and reads it\n        // back to arm `app.current_org` before any FORCE-RLS table read.\n        let org = current_org()?;\n        let payload = MessageNotifyPayload::from_notification(notification, org).to_json_bytes()?;\n        Self::validate_payload_size_for_test(&payload)?;\n        let payload = String::from_utf8(payload).map_err(|err| {\n            serde_json::Error::io(std::io::Error::new(std::io::ErrorKind::InvalidData, err))\n        })?;\n\n        sqlx::query(\"SELECT pg_notify($1, $2)\")\n            .bind(MESSAGE_POSTED_CHANNEL)\n            .bind(payload)\n            // rls-arming: ok pg_notify is not a tenant-table read\n            .execute(&self.pool)\n            .await?;\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    pub fn validate_payload_size_for_test(bytes: &[u8]) -> Result<(), NotifyPayloadError> {\n        validate_payload_size(bytes)\n    }\n}\n\nimpl MessageNotifier for PostgresMessageNotifier {\n    fn message_posted(&self, notification: MessagePostedNotification) -> MessageNotifyFuture<'_> {\n        Box::pin(async move {\n            if let Err(err) = self.notify_message_posted(notification).await {\n                tracing::error!(error = %err, \"failed to publish messenger realtime notification\");\n            }\n        })\n    }\n}\n\nfn validate_payload_size(bytes: &[u8]) -> Result<(), NotifyPayloadError> {\n    if bytes.len() >= NOTIFY_PAYLOAD_LIMIT_BYTES {\n        Err(NotifyPayloadError::PayloadTooLarge {\n            size: bytes.len(),\n            limit: NOTIFY_PAYLOAD_LIMIT_BYTES,\n        })\n    } else {\n        Ok(())\n    }\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Serialize, Deserialize)]\n#[serde(tag = \"type\", rename_all = \"snake_case\")]\npub enum RealtimeEvent {\n    MessagePosted { message: MessageSummary },\n}\n\nimpl RealtimeEvent {\n    fn message_id(&self) -> MessageId {\n        match self {\n            Self::MessagePosted { message } => message.id,\n        }\n    }\n\n    fn cursor(&self) -> MessageCursor {\n        match self {\n            Self::MessagePosted { message } => MessageCursor {\n                sent_at: message.sent_at,\n                id: message.id,\n            },\n        }\n    }\n\n    fn branch_id(&self) -> BranchId {\n        match self {\n            Self::MessagePosted { message } => message.branch_id,\n        }\n    }\n\n    fn thread_id(&self) -> ThreadId {\n        match self {\n            Self::MessagePosted { message } => MessageId,\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq)]\npub struct RealtimeHubConfig {\n    pub connection_buffer: usize,\n}\n\nimpl Default for RealtimeHubConfig {\n    fn default() -> Self {\n        Self {\n            connection_buffer: DEFAULT_CONNECTION_BUFFER,\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq)]\npub struct RealtimePrincipal {\n    pub user_id: UserId,\n    pub Replay reads run in a background task with no request\n    /// context, so this org arms `app.current_org` for the subscriber's own\n    /// FORCE-RLS reads.\n    pub org_id: OrgId,\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Serialize, Deserialize)]\n#[serde(rename_all = \"snake_case\")]\npub enum DisconnectReason {\n    LaggingConsumer,\n    ReplayFailed,\n    ServerShutdown,\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct DisconnectNotice {\n    pub reason: DisconnectReason,\n    pub resume_after: Option<MessageId>,\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug)]\npub struct RealtimeConnection {\n    id: uuid::Uuid,\n    events_rx: mpsc::Receiver<RealtimeEvent>,\n    disconnect_rx: mpsc::UnboundedReceiver<DisconnectNotice>,\n}\n\nimpl RealtimeConnection {\n    #[must_use]\n    pub fn id(&self) -> uuid::Uuid {\n        self.id\n    }\n\n    pub async fn recv(&mut self) -> Option<RealtimeEvent> {\n        self.events_rx.recv().await\n    }\n\n    pub async fn disconnect(&mut self) -> Option<DisconnectNotice> {\n        self.disconnect_rx.recv().await\n    }\n\n    fn into_parts(\n        self,\n    ) -> (\n        uuid::Uuid,\n        mpsc::Receiver<RealtimeEvent>,\n        mpsc::UnboundedReceiver<DisconnectNotice>,\n    ) {\n        (self.id, self.events_rx, self.disconnect_rx)\n    }\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug)]\nstruct ConnectionSlot {\n    principal: RealtimePrincipal,\n    events_tx: mpsc::Sender<RealtimeEvent>,\n    disconnect_tx: mpsc::UnboundedSender<DisconnectNotice>,\n    delivery_state: ConnectionDeliveryState,\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug)]\nenum ConnectionDeliveryState {\n    Live,\n    Replaying {\n        buffered_events: Vec<RealtimeEvent>,\n        replay_cursor: Option<MessageCursor>,\n    },\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug)]\npub struct PgRealtimeHub {\n    pool: Option<PgPool>,\n    config: RealtimeHubConfig,\n    connections: Mutex<HashMap<uuid::Uuid, ConnectionSlot>>,\n}\n\nimpl PgRealtimeHub {\n    #[must_use]\n    pub fn new(pool: PgPool, config: RealtimeHubConfig) -> Self {\n        Self {\n            pool: Some(pool),\n            config,\n            connections: Mutex::new(HashMap::new()),\n        }\n    }\n\n    #[must_use]\n    pub fn for_tests(config: RealtimeHubConfig) -> Self {\n        Self {\n            pool: None,\n            config,\n            connections: Mutex::new(HashMap::new()),\n        }\n    }\n\n    pub async fn connect(\n        self: &Arc<Self>,\n        principal: RealtimePrincipal,\n        last_message_id: Option<MessageId>,\n    ) -> Result<RealtimeConnection, RealtimeError> {\n        if last_message_id.is_some() && self.pool.is_none() {\n            return Err(RealtimeError::DatabaseNotConfigured);\n        }\n\n        let capacity = self.config.connection_buffer.max(1);\n        let (events_tx, events_rx) = mpsc::channel(capacity);\n        let (disconnect_tx, disconnect_rx) = mpsc::unbounded_channel();\n        let id = uuid::Uuid::new_v4();\n        let delivery_state = if last_message_id.is_some() {\n            ConnectionDeliveryState::Replaying {\n                buffered_events: Vec::new(),\n                replay_cursor: None,\n            }\n        } else {\n            ConnectionDeliveryState::Live\n        };\n        self.connections.lock().await.insert(\n            id,\n            ConnectionSlot {\n                principal: principal.clone(),\n                events_tx,\n                disconnect_tx,\n                delivery_state,\n            },\n        );\n\n        if let Some(last_message_id) = last_message_id {\n            let hub = Arc::clone(self);\n            tokio::spawn(async move {\n                hub.run_replay(id, principal, last_message_id).await;\n            });\n        }\n\n        Ok(RealtimeConnection {\n            id,\n            events_rx,\n            disconnect_rx,\n        })\n    }\n\n    pub async fn connection_count(&self) -> usize {\n        self.connections.lock().await.len()\n    }\n\n    pub async fn remove_connection(&self, connection_id: uuid::Uuid) {\n        self.connections.lock().await.remove(&connection_id);\n    }\n\n    pub async fn dispatch_local_for_test(\n        &self,\n        org: OrgId,\n        event: RealtimeEvent,\n    ) -> Result<(), RealtimeError> {\n        self.dispatch_event(org, event, None).await\n    }\n\n    pub async fn shutdown(&self) {\n        let mut connections = self.connections.lock().await;\n        for (_, slot) in connections.drain() {\n            let _ = slot.disconnect_tx.send(DisconnectNotice {\n                reason: DisconnectReason::ServerShutdown,\n                resume_after: None,\n            });\n        }\n    }\n\n    pub async fn start_postgres_listener(\n        self: Arc<Self>,\n    ) -> Result<PostgresBridgeHandle, RealtimeError> {\n        let pool = self\n            .pool\n            .as_ref()\n            .ok_or(RealtimeError::DatabaseNotConfigured)?\n            .clone();\n        let mut listener = PgListener::connect_with(&pool).await?;\n        listener.listen(MESSAGE_POSTED_CHANNEL).await?;\n        let (shutdown_tx, mut shutdown_rx) = watch::channel(false);\n        let hub = Arc::clone(&self);\n\n        tokio::spawn(async move {\n            loop {\n                tokio::select! {\n                    changed = shutdown_rx.changed() => {\n                        if changed.is_err() || *shutdown_rx.borrow() {\n                            break;\n                        }\n                    }\n                    notification = listener.recv() => {\n                        match notification {\n                            Ok(notification) => {\n                                if notification.channel() == MESSAGE_POSTED_CHANNEL\n                                    && let Err(err) = hub.handle_notify_payload(notification.payload()).await\n                                {\n                                    tracing::warn!(error = %err, \"failed to handle messenger realtime notification\");\n                                }\n                            }\n                            Err(err) => {\n                                tracing::warn!(error = %err, \"Postgres realtime listener failed; retrying\");\n                                tokio::time::sleep(Duration::from_millis(100)).await;\n                            }\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        });\n\n        Ok(PostgresBridgeHandle { shutdown_tx })\n    }\n\n    async fn handle_notify_payload(&self, payload: &str) -> Result<(), RealtimeError> {\n        let payload = MessageNotifyPayload::from_json_bytes(payload.as_bytes())?;\n        // The listener has no request context; the org rides on the payload and\n        // scopes every FORCE-RLS read triggered by this notification.\n        let org = payload.org_id;\n        let message = self\n            .fetch_message(org, payload.message_id, payload.thread_id)\n            .await?;\n        self.dispatch_event(org, RealtimeEvent::MessagePosted { message }, None)\n            .await\n    }\n\n    async fn run_replay(\n        self: Arc<Self>,\n        connection_id: uuid::Uuid,\n        principal: RealtimePrincipal,\n        last_message_id: MessageId,\n    ) {\n        let result = async {\n            self.replay_after(connection_id, &principal, last_message_id)\n                .await?;\n            self.finish_replay(connection_id).await\n        }\n        .await;\n\n        if let Err(err) = result {\n            tracing::warn!(error = %err, \"realtime replay failed\");\n            let resume_after = self.replay_resume_after(connection_id).await;\n            self.disconnect_connection(connection_id, DisconnectReason::ReplayFailed, resume_after)\n                .await;\n        }\n    }\n\n    async fn replay_after(\n        &self,\n        connection_id: uuid::Uuid,\n        principal: &RealtimePrincipal,\n        last_message_id: MessageId,\n    ) -> Result<(), RealtimeError> {\n        let pool = self\n            .pool\n            .as_ref()\n            .ok_or(RealtimeError::DatabaseNotConfigured)?;\n        // Replay runs in a spawned task with no request context, so the org is\n        // carried from the authenticated subscriber session (`principal.org_id`)\n        // and arms `app.current_org` for every FORCE-RLS read below.\n        let org = principal.org_id;\n        let last_message_uuid = *last_message_id.as_uuid();\n        let cursor_row = with_org_conn::<_, _, RealtimeError>(pool, org, move |tx| {\n            Box::pin(async move {\n                Ok(\n                    sqlx::query(\"SELECT sent_at, id FROM messenger_messages WHERE id = $1\")\n                        .bind(last_message_uuid)\n                        .fetch_optional(tx.as_mut())\n                        .await?,\n                )\n            })\n        })\n        .await?;\n        let Some(cursor) = cursor_row else {\n            return Ok(());\n        };\n        let mut cursor = MessageCursor {\n            sent_at: cursor.try_get(\"sent_at\")?,\n            id: MessageId::from_uuid(cursor.try_get(\"id\")?),\n        };\n\n        loop {\n            let cursor_sent_at = cursor.sent_at;\n            let cursor_id = *cursor.id.as_uuid();\n            let branch_scope = principal.branch_scope.clone();\n            let user_uuid = *principal.user_id.as_uuid();\n            let rows = with_org_conn::<_, _, RealtimeError>(pool, org, move |tx| {\n                Box::pin(async move {\n                    let mut builder = message_select_builder();\n                    builder.push(\n                        r#\"\n                JOIN messenger_thread_members tm\n                  ON tm.thread_id = m.thread_id\n                 AND tm.user_id =\n                \"#,\n                    );\n                    builder.push_bind(user_uuid);\n                    builder.push(\" WHERE (m.sent_at, m.id) > (\");\n                    builder.push_bind(cursor_sent_at);\n                    builder.push(\", \");\n                    builder.push_bind(cursor_id);\n                    builder.push(\")\");\n                    push_scope_filter(&mut builder, \"m.branch_id\", &branch_scope);\n                    builder.push(\" GROUP BY m.id ORDER BY m.sent_at ASC, m.id ASC LIMIT \");\n                    builder.push_bind(REPLAY_PAGE_SIZE);\n                    Ok(builder.build().fetch_all(tx.as_mut()).await?)\n                })\n            })\n            .await?;\n            if rows.is_empty() {\n                break;\n            }\n\n            let row_count = rows.len();\n            for row in rows {\n                let message = message_summary_from_row(&row)?;\n                cursor = MessageCursor {\n                    sent_at: message.sent_at,\n                    id: message.id,\n                };\n                let event = RealtimeEvent::MessagePosted { message };\n                if !self.send_replay_event(connection_id, event).await? {\n                    return Ok(());\n                }\n            }\n\n            if row_count < usize::try_from(REPLAY_PAGE_SIZE).unwrap_or(usize::MAX) {\n                break;\n            }\n        }\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    async fn fetch_message(\n        &self,\n        org: OrgId,\n        message_id: MessageId,\n        thread_id: ThreadId,\n    ) -> Result<MessageSummary, RealtimeError> {\n        let pool = self\n            .pool\n            .as_ref()\n            .ok_or(RealtimeError::DatabaseNotConfigured)?;\n        let message_uuid = *message_id.as_uuid();\n        let thread_uuid = *thread_id.as_uuid();\n        // The org is carried from the NOTIFY payload; arm it so this read sees\n        // the publishing tenant's FORCE-RLS rows.\n        with_org_conn::<_, _, RealtimeError>(pool, org, move |tx| {\n            Box::pin(async move {\n                let mut builder = message_select_builder();\n                builder.push(\" WHERE m.id = \");\n                builder.push_bind(message_uuid);\n                builder.push(\" AND m.thread_id = \");\n                builder.push_bind(thread_uuid);\n                builder.push(\" GROUP BY m.id\");\n                let row = builder.build().fetch_one(tx.as_mut()).await?;\n                message_summary_from_row(&row).map_err(|err| RealtimeError::Db(DbError::Sqlx(err)))\n            })\n        })\n        .await\n    }\n\n    async fn dispatch_event(\n        &self,\n        org: OrgId,\n        event: RealtimeEvent,\n        authorized_users: Option<HashSet<UserId>>,\n    ) -> Result<(), RealtimeError> {\n        let branch_id = event.branch_id();\n        let candidate_users = if authorized_users.is_some() || self.pool.is_none() {\n            authorized_users\n        } else {\n            let candidates = {\n                let connections = self.connections.lock().await;\n                connections\n                    .values()\n                    .filter(|slot| slot.principal.branch_scope.allows(branch_id))\n                    .map(|slot| slot.principal.user_id)\n                    .collect::<Vec<_>>()\n            };\n            Some(\n                self.authorized_thread_members(org, event.thread_id(), candidates)\n                    .await?,\n            )\n        };\n\n        let targets = {\n            let connections = self.connections.lock().await;\n            connections\n                .iter()\n                .filter(|(_, slot)| slot.principal.branch_scope.allows(branch_id))\n                .filter(|(_, slot)| {\n                    candidate_users\n                        .as_ref()\n                        .is_none_or(|users| users.contains(&slot.principal.user_id))\n                })\n                .map(|(id, _)| *id)\n                .collect::<Vec<_>>()\n        };\n\n        for connection_id in targets {\n            self.dispatch_to_connection(connection_id, event.clone(), None)\n                .await;\n        }\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    async fn send_replay_event(\n        &self,\n        connection_id: uuid::Uuid,\n        event: RealtimeEvent,\n    ) -> Result<bool, RealtimeError> {\n        let cursor = event.cursor();\n        let events_tx = {\n            let connections = self.connections.lock().await;\n            let Some(slot) = connections.get(&connection_id) else {\n                return Ok(false);\n            };\n            slot.events_tx.clone()\n        };\n\n        match tokio::time::timeout(REPLAY_SEND_TIMEOUT, events_tx.send(event)).await {\n            Ok(Ok(())) => {\n                self.mark_replay_cursor(connection_id, cursor).await;\n                Ok(true)\n            }\n            Ok(Err(_)) => {\n                self.remove_connection(connection_id).await;\n                Err(RealtimeError::ConnectionClosed)\n            }\n            Err(_) => {\n                let resume_after = self.replay_resume_after(connection_id).await;\n                self.disconnect_connection(\n                    connection_id,\n                    DisconnectReason::LaggingConsumer,\n                    resume_after,\n                )\n                .await;\n                Err(RealtimeError::ReplayTimedOut {\n                    timeout: REPLAY_SEND_TIMEOUT,\n                })\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    async fn finish_replay(&self, connection_id: uuid::Uuid) -> Result<(), RealtimeError> {\n        loop {\n            let events = {\n                let mut connections = self.connections.lock().await;\n                let Some(slot) = connections.get_mut(&connection_id) else {\n                    return Ok(());\n                };\n                match &mut slot.delivery_state {\n                    ConnectionDeliveryState::Live => return Ok(()),\n                    ConnectionDeliveryState::Replaying {\n                        buffered_events,\n                        replay_cursor,\n                    } => {\n                        if buffered_events.is_empty() {\n                            slot.delivery_state = ConnectionDeliveryState::Live;\n                            return Ok(());\n                        }\n                        let replay_cursor = *replay_cursor;\n                        let mut events = std::mem::take(buffered_events);\n                        events.sort_by_key(RealtimeEvent::cursor);\n                        let mut seen = HashSet::new();\n                        events.retain(|event| {\n                            let cursor = event.cursor();\n                            replay_cursor.is_none_or(|replay_cursor| cursor > replay_cursor)\n                                && seen.insert(event.message_id())\n                        });\n                        events\n                    }\n                }\n            };\n\n            for event in events {\n                if !self.send_replay_event(connection_id, event).await? {\n                    return Ok(());\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    async fn mark_replay_cursor(&self, connection_id: uuid::Uuid, cursor: MessageCursor) {\n        let mut connections = self.connections.lock().await;\n        if let Some(slot) = connections.get_mut(&connection_id)\n            && let ConnectionDeliveryState::Replaying { replay_cursor, .. } =\n                &mut slot.delivery_state\n        {\n            *replay_cursor = Some(cursor);\n        }\n    }\n\n    async fn replay_resume_after(&self, connection_id: uuid::Uuid) -> Option<MessageId> {\n        let connections = self.connections.lock().await;\n        connections\n            .get(&connection_id)\n            .and_then(|slot| match &slot.delivery_state {\n                ConnectionDeliveryState::Live => None,\n                ConnectionDeliveryState::Replaying { replay_cursor, .. } => {\n                    replay_cursor.map(|cursor| cursor.id)\n                }\n            })\n    }\n\n    async fn disconnect_connection(\n        &self,\n        connection_id: uuid::Uuid,\n        reason: DisconnectReason,\n        resume_after: Option<MessageId>,\n    ) {\n        let mut connections = self.connections.lock().await;\n        if let Some(slot) = connections.remove(&connection_id) {\n            let _ = slot.disconnect_tx.send(DisconnectNotice {\n                reason,\n                resume_after,\n            });\n        }\n    }\n\n    async fn dispatch_to_connection(\n        &self,\n        connection_id: uuid::Uuid,\n        event: RealtimeEvent,\n        resume_after: Option<MessageId>,\n    ) {\n        let mut connections = self.connections.lock().await;\n        let Some(slot) = connections.get_mut(&connection_id) else {\n            return;\n        };\n\n        let mut disconnect_resume_after = None;\n        match &mut slot.delivery_state {\n            ConnectionDeliveryState::Live => {\n                if slot.events_tx.try_send(event).is_err() {\n                    disconnect_resume_after = Some(resume_after);\n                }\n            }\n            ConnectionDeliveryState::Replaying {\n                buffered_events,\n                replay_cursor,\n            } => {\n                if buffered_events.len() >= self.config.connection_buffer.max(1) {\n                    disconnect_resume_after =\n                        Some(replay_cursor.map(|cursor| cursor.id).or(resume_after));\n                } else {\n                    buffered_events.push(event);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        if let Some(resume_after) = disconnect_resume_after\n            && let Some(slot) = connections.remove(&connection_id)\n        {\n            let _ = slot.disconnect_tx.send(DisconnectNotice {\n                reason: DisconnectReason::LaggingConsumer,\n                resume_after,\n            });\n        }\n    }\n\n    async fn authorized_thread_members(\n        &self,\n        org: OrgId,\n        thread_id: ThreadId,\n        candidates: Vec<UserId>,\n    ) -> Result<HashSet<UserId>, RealtimeError> {\n        let Some(pool) = &self.pool else {\n            return Ok(candidates.into_iter().collect());\n        };\n        if candidates.is_empty() {\n            return Ok(HashSet::new());\n        }\n        let candidate_ids = candidates\n            .into_iter()\n            .map(|user_id| *user_id.as_uuid())\n            .collect::<Vec<_>>();\n        let thread_uuid = *thread_id.as_uuid();\n        // The org is carried from the NOTIFY payload; arm it so the membership\n        // read sees the publishing tenant's FORCE-RLS rows.\n        let rows: Vec<uuid::Uuid> = with_org_conn::<_, _, RealtimeError>(pool, org, move |tx| {\n            Box::pin(async move {\n                Ok(sqlx::query_scalar(\n                    r#\"\n            SELECT user_id\n            FROM messenger_thread_members\n            WHERE thread_id = $1\n              AND user_id = ANY($2)\n            \"#,\n                )\n                .bind(thread_uuid)\n                .bind(candidate_ids)\n                .fetch_all(tx.as_mut())\n                .await?)\n            })\n        })\n        .await?;\n\n        Ok(rows.into_iter().map(UserId::from_uuid).collect())\n    }\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct PostgresBridgeHandle {\n    shutdown_tx: watch::Sender<bool>,\n}\n\nimpl PostgresBridgeHandle {\n    pub fn shutdown(&self) {\n        let _ = self.shutdown_tx.send(true);\n    }\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct RealtimeRestState {\n    hub: Arc<PgRealtimeHub>,\n    jwt_verifier: Option<JwtVerifier>,\n}\n\nimpl RealtimeRestState {\n    #[must_use]\n    pub fn new(hub: Arc<PgRealtimeHub>, jwt_verifier: Option<JwtVerifier>) -> Self {\n        Self { hub, jwt_verifier }\n    }\n\n    #[must_use]\n    pub fn hub(&self) -> &Arc<PgRealtimeHub> {\n        &self.hub\n    }\n}\n\npub fn router(state: RealtimeRestState) -> Router {\n    Router::new()\n        .route(\"/api/v1/ws\", get(websocket_handler))\n        .with_state(state)\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Deserialize)]\nstruct WsQuery {\n    last_message_id: Option<MessageId>,\n}\n\nasync fn websocket_handler(\n    State(state): State<RealtimeRestState>,\n    headers: HeaderMap,\n    Query(query): Query<WsQuery>,\n    ws: WebSocketUpgrade,\n) -> Result<Response, RealtimeApiError> {\n    let principal = principal_from_headers(&state, &headers)?;\n    Ok(ws\n        // Browser clients carry the bearer token as a `Sec-WebSocket-Protocol`\n        // subprotocol pair (`bearer, <token>`); the WebSocket handshake REQUIRES\n        // the server to echo one offered subprotocol, so select `bearer` to\n        // complete the handshake (without this the browser aborts with \"Sent\n        // non-empty 'Sec-WebSocket-Protocol' header but no response was received\").\n        .protocols([\"bearer\"])\n        .on_upgrade(move |socket| {\n            websocket_session(state, principal, query.last_message_id, socket)\n        })\n        .into_response())\n}\n\nasync fn websocket_session(\n    state: RealtimeRestState,\n    principal: RealtimePrincipal,\n    last_message_id: Option<MessageId>,\n    mut socket: WebSocket,\n) {\n    let connection = match state.hub.connect(principal, last_message_id).await {\n        Ok(connection) => connection,\n        Err(err) => {\n            tracing::warn!(error = %err, \"realtime websocket connect failed\");\n            let _ = socket\n                .send(Message::Close(Some(CloseFrame {\n                    code: 1011,\n                    reason: \"realtime unavailable\".into(),\n                })))\n                .await;\n            return;\n        }\n    };\n    let (connection_id, mut events_rx, mut disconnect_rx) = connection.into_parts();\n\n    loop {\n        tokio::select! {\n            notice = disconnect_rx.recv() => {\n                if let Some(notice) = notice {\n                    let (code, reason) = close_frame_for_notice(&notice);\n                    let _ = socket\n                        .send(Message::Close(Some(CloseFrame { code, reason: reason.into() })))\n                        .await;\n                }\n                break;\n            }\n            event = events_rx.recv() => {\n                let Some(event) = event else {\n                    break;\n                };\n                match serde_json::to_string(&event) {\n                    Ok(json) => {\n                        if socket.send(Message::Text(json.into())).await.is_err() {\n                            break;\n                        }\n                    }\n                    Err(err) => {\n                        tracing::error!(error = %err, \"failed to serialize realtime event\");\n                        break;\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n            incoming = socket.recv() => {\n                match incoming {\n                    Some(Ok(Message::Close(_))) | None => break,\n                    Some(Ok(_)) => {}\n                    Some(Err(err)) => {\n                        tracing::debug!(error = %err, \"websocket receive failed\");\n                        break;\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    state.hub.remove_connection(connection_id).await;\n}\n\nfn close_frame_for_notice(notice: &DisconnectNotice) -> (u16, String) {\n    match notice.reason {\n        DisconnectReason::LaggingConsumer => (\n            1013,\n            \"lagging_consumer; reconnect with last_message_id cursor\".to_owned(),\n        ),\n        DisconnectReason::ReplayFailed => (\n            1011,\n            \"replay_failed; reconnect with last_message_id cursor\".to_owned(),\n        ),\n        DisconnectReason::ServerShutdown => (1001, \"server_shutdown\".to_owned()),\n    }\n}\n\nfn principal_from_headers(\n    state: &RealtimeRestState,\n    headers: &HeaderMap,\n) -> Result<RealtimePrincipal, RealtimeApiError> {\n    let verifier = state.jwt_verifier.as_ref().ok_or_else(|| {\n        RealtimeApiError::new(\n            StatusCode::SERVICE_UNAVAILABLE,\n            \"unavailable\",\n            \"JWT verification is not configured for realtime\",\n        )\n    })?;\n    let token = bearer_token(headers)?;\n    let claims = verifier\n        .verify_access_token(token)\n        .map_err(|_| RealtimeApiError::unauthorized(\"invalid bearer token\"))?;\n    principal_from_claims(claims)\n}\n\nfn bearer_token(headers: &HeaderMap) -> Result<&str, RealtimeApiError> {\n    if let Some(token) = authorization_bearer_token(headers)? {\n        return Ok(token);\n    }\n    if let Some(token) = websocket_protocol_bearer_token(headers)? {\n        return Ok(token);\n    }\n    Err(RealtimeApiError::unauthorized(\"missing bearer token\"))\n}\n\nfn authorization_bearer_token(headers: &HeaderMap) -> Result<Option<&str>, RealtimeApiError> {\n    let Some(header_value) = headers.get(header::AUTHORIZATION) else {\n        return Ok(None);\n    };\n    let header_value = header_value\n        .to_str()\n        .map_err(|_| RealtimeApiError::unauthorized(\"invalid authorization header\"))?;\n    let token = header_value\n        .strip_prefix(\"Bearer \")\n        .filter(|token| !token.trim().is_empty())\n        .ok_or_else(|| {\n            RealtimeApiError::unauthorized(\"authorization header must use Bearer scheme\")\n        })?;\n    Ok(Some(token))\n}\n\nfn websocket_protocol_bearer_token(headers: &HeaderMap) -> Result<Option<&str>, RealtimeApiError> {\n    let Some(header_value) = headers.get(header::SEC_WEBSOCKET_PROTOCOL) else {\n        return Ok(None);\n    };\n    let header_value = header_value\n        .to_str()\n        .map_err(|_| RealtimeApiError::unauthorized(\"invalid websocket protocol header\"))?;\n    let protocols = header_value.split(',').map(str::trim).collect::<Vec<_>>();\n    let token = protocols\n        .windows(2)\n        .find_map(|pair| (pair[0] == \"bearer\" && !pair[1].is_empty()).then_some(pair[1]));\n    Ok(token)\n}\n\nfn principal_from_claims(claims: AccessClaims) -> Result<RealtimePrincipal, RealtimeApiError> {\n    let user_id = UserId::from_str(&claims.sub)\n        .map_err(|_| RealtimeApiError::unauthorized(\"token subject is not a valid user id\"))?;\n    // The realtime router runs OUTSIDE the tenant org middleware, so the\n    // subscriber's org is taken straight from the verified JWT `org` claim and\n    // carried on the principal for replay reads.\n    let org_id = OrgId::from_str(&claims.org)\n        .map_err(|_| RealtimeApiError::unauthorized(\"token contains an invalid org id\"))?;\n    let has_global_scope = claims\n        .roles\n        .iter()\n        .any(|role| matches!(role.as_str(), \"SUPER_ADMIN\" | \"EXECUTIVE\"));\n    let branch_scope = if has_global_scope {\n        BranchScope::All\n    } else {\n        let branches = claims\n            .branches\n            .iter()\n            .map(|branch| {\n                BranchId::from_str(branch).map_err(|_| {\n                    RealtimeApiError::unauthorized(\"token contains an invalid branch id\")\n                })\n            })\n            .collect::<Result<_, _>>()?;\n        BranchScope::Branches(branches)\n    };\n\n    Ok(RealtimePrincipal {\n        user_id,\n        branch_scope,\n        org_id,\n    })\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Serialize)]\nstruct ErrorBody {\n    error: ErrorPayload,\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Serialize)]\nstruct ErrorPayload {\n    code: &'static str,\n    message: String,\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug)]\nstruct RealtimeApiError {\n    status: StatusCode,\n    code: &'static str,\n    message: String,\n}\n\nimpl RealtimeApiError {\n    fn new(status: StatusCode, code: &'static str, message: impl Into<String>) -> Self {\n        Self {\n            status,\n            code,\n            message: message.into(),\n        }\n    }\n\n    fn unauthorized(message: impl Into<String>) -> Self {\n        Self::new(StatusCode::UNAUTHORIZED, \"unauthorized\", message)\n    }\n}\n\nimpl IntoResponse for RealtimeApiError {\n    fn into_response(self) -> Response {\n        (\n            self.status,\n            Json(ErrorBody {\n                error: ErrorPayload {\n                    code: self.code,\n                    message: self.message,\n                },\n            }),\n        )\n            .into_response()\n    }\n}\n\nfn message_select_builder() -> QueryBuilder<Postgres> {\n    QueryBuilder::<Postgres>::new(\n        r#\"\n        SELECT m.id, m.thread_id, m.branch_id, m.sender_id, m.body,\n               m.sent_at, m.created_at,\n               COALESCE(\n                   array_agg(a.evidence_id ORDER BY a.sort_order)\n                       FILTER (WHERE a.evidence_id IS NOT NULL),\n                   ARRAY[]::uuid[]\n               ) AS attachment_evidence_ids\n        FROM messenger_messages m\n        LEFT JOIN messenger_message_attachments a ON a.message_id = m.id\n        \"#,\n    )\n}\n\nfn message_summary_from_row(row: &sqlx::postgres::PgRow) -> Result<MessageSummary, sqlx::Error> {\n    let attachment_ids: Vec<uuid::Uuid> = row.try_get(\"attachment_evidence_ids\")?;\n    Ok(MessageSummary {\n        id: MessageId::from_uuid(row.try_get(\"id\")?),\n        thread_id: ThreadId::from_uuid(row.try_get(\"thread_id\")?),\n        branch_id: BranchId::from_uuid(row.try_get(\"branch_id\")?),\n        sender_id: UserId::from_uuid(row.try_get(\"sender_id\")?),\n        body: row.try_get(\"body\")?,\n        attachment_evidence_ids: attachment_ids\n            .into_iter()\n            .map(mnt_kernel_core::EvidenceId::from_uuid)\n            .collect(),\n        sent_at: row.try_get(\"sent_at\")?,\n        created_at: row.try_get(\"created_at\")?,\n    })\n}\n\nfn push_scope_filter(builder: &mut QueryBuilder<Postgres>, column: &str, scope: &BranchScope) {\n    match scope {\n        BranchScope::All => {}\n        BranchScope::Branches(branches) if branches.is_empty() => {\n            builder.push(\" AND false\");\n        }\n        BranchScope::Branches(branches) => {\n            let branch_ids: Vec<uuid::Uuid> =\n                branches.iter().map(|branch| *branch.as_uuid()).collect();\n            builder.push(\" AND \");\n            builder.push(column);\n            builder.push(\" = ANY(\");\n            builder.push_bind(branch_ids);\n            builder.push(\")\");\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod auth_tests {\n    use super::*;\n    use axum::http::HeaderValue;\n\n    #[test]\n    fn bearer_token_accepts_authorization_header() {\n        let mut headers = HeaderMap::new();\n        headers.insert(\n            header::AUTHORIZATION,\n            HeaderValue::from_static(\"Bearer native-token\"),\n        );\n\n        assert_eq!(bearer_token(&headers).expect(\"token\"), \"native-token\");\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn bearer_token_accepts_websocket_subprotocol_pair() {\n        let mut headers = HeaderMap::new();\n        headers.insert(\n
